    <title>Document</title>
</head>
<body>

</body>
</html>

</body>

-----------------------------------------------------2. Bootstrap Fundamentals - Part 1------------------------------------------

##################################################1. Containers ##############################################
<div class="container">container</div>
Centered automatically.(content গুলো  automatically Centered হবে।)

<div class="container-sm">Small container</div>
sm: 540px
Fixed-width container starting at small (sm) breakpoint (≥576px).(screen size 576px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content গুলো 546px এ বসবে।content গুলো  automatically Centered হবে। )

<div class="container-md">Medium container</div>
md: 720px
Fixed-width container starting at medium (md) breakpoint (≥768px).(screen size 768px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content গুলো 720px এ বসবে।content গুলো  automatically Centered হবে। )

<div class="container-lg">Large container</div>
lg: 960px
Fixed-width container starting at large (lg) breakpoint (≥992px).(screen size 992px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content গুলো 960px এ বসবে।content গুলো  automatically Centered হবে। )

<div class="container-xl">Extra-large container</div>
xl: 1140px
Fixed-width container starting at extra-large (xl) breakpoint (≥1200px).(screen size 1200px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content গুলো 1140px এ বসবে।content গুলো  automatically Centered হবে। )

<div class="container-xxl">Extra-extra-large container</div>
xxl: 1320px
Fixed-width container starting at extra-extra-large (xxl) breakpoint (≥1400px).(screen size 1400px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content গুলো 1320px এ বসবে।content গুলো  automatically Centered হবে। )

<div class="container-fluid">Full-width container</div>
fluid: 100%
Full-width container spanning the entire width.(পুরো জায়গা নিয়ে নিবে।)

##################################################2. Typography ##############################################
1. Headings and Typography:

h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6: Default HTML headings for different text sizes.

.h1 to .h6: Apply heading styles to any element (e.g., <p>).(Bootstrap এর class use করে Bold হবে।)

.display-1 to .display-6: Larger, prominent headings for hero sections.(নরমাল Bold এর চেয়ে বেশী Bold হবে।)


2. Text Utilities:

.lead: Styles a paragraph with increased font size and lighter weight for emphasis.

.blockquote: Styles a blockquote with indentation for quotes.



3. Font Weight & Style:

.fw-bold to .fw-lighter: Adjusts text weight from bold to light.
.fst-italic: Applies italic style.
.fst-normal: Resets to normal font style.



4. Line Height:

.lh-1,.lh-2 .lh-sm, .lh-base, .lh-lg: Controls line height (1x, small, base, large).



5. Text Transform:

.text-lowercase: Converts text to lowercase.
.text-uppercase: Converts text to uppercase.
.text-capitalize: Capitalizes the first letter of each word.


6. Text Alignment:(container এ text কোথায় বসবে তা সেট করা যায়।)

.text-start, .text-center, .text-end: Aligns text to the left, center, or right.


text-sm-end==>screen size 576px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content/text গুলো শেষে বসবে।
text-md-end==>screen size 768px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content/text গুলো শেষে বসবে।
text-lg-end==>screen size 992px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content/text গুলো শেষে বসবে।
text-xl-end==>screen size 1200px এর উপরে গেলে আউটপুট এ content/text গুলো শেষে বসবে।
Responsive Alignment: .text-sm-end, .text-md-end, .text-lg-end, .text-xl-end align text based on screen size breakpoints.


<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />

-------------------------------------------3. Display & Position---------------------------------------

<div class="position-static">...</div>
Default positioning (no special positioning applied).
normally যেখানে বসার কথা সেখানে বসবে।

<div class="position-relative">...</div>
Positioned relative to its normal position. Child elements with absolute positioning use this as their reference.
(যেখানে বসার কথা সেখানে বসবে তবে child element বসবে relative কে ফলো করে।)

<div class="position-absolute">...</div>
Positioned relative to the nearest positioned ancestor (relative, absolute, or fixed).
(এক্ষেত্রে relative parent element এর child হিসেবে absolute ব্যবহার করতে হয়)

<div class="position-fixed">...</div>
Positioned relative to the viewport and remains in place during scrolling.
(ফিক্সড পজিশন হিসেবে element বসবে। যেখানে element বসাব সেখানে বসবে।)

		<!-- Relative and Absolute Positioning -->
        <div class="position-relative bg-primary text-white p-4 mb-4" style="height: 150px;">

            <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0 bg-danger text-white p-2">
                I'm positioned absolutely within the relative container.
            </div>
        </div>

<div class="position-sticky">...</div>
(Sticks to a defined offset (top, bottom, etc.) as you scroll but only within its parent container.)
(page scroll করলে যেখানে সেট করব সেখানে ফিক্সড হবে।)
(তবে parent element এর viewport full হতে হবে।)

 <!-- Parent -->
<div class="container-md">
    <!-- Sticky Positioning -->
    <div class="position-sticky top-0 bg-warning text-dark p-3" style="z-index: 1020;">
        <p class="mb-0">I stick to the top when scrolling!</p>
    </div>
</div>



(element কোথায় সেট করব তার পজিশন ফিক্সড করা হয় top,start,bottom,end এর মাধ্যমে।)
top - for the vertical top position
start - for the horizontal left position (in LTR)
bottom - for the vertical bottom position
end - for the horizontal right position (in LTR)
Where position is one of:

0 - for 0 edge position
50 - for 50% edge position
100 - for 100% edge position

		top-0 end-0(top-right corner element set হবে।)
		top-0 start-0(top-left corner element set হবে।)
		bottom-0 start-0(bottom-left corner element set হবে।)
		bottom-0 end-0(bottom-right corner element set হবে।)
		
		<!-- Relative and Absolute Positioning -->
        <div class="position-relative bg-primary text-white p-4 mb-4" style="height: 150px;">

            <div class="position-absolute top-0 end-0 bg-danger text-white p-2">
                I'm positioned absolutely within the relative container.
            </div>
        </div>




Center elements:
In addition, you can also center the elements with the transform utility class .translate-middle.
This class applies the transformations translateX(-50%) and translateY(-50%) to the element which, in combination with the edge positioning utilities, allows you to absolute center an element.
(translate-middle :
	top-0 start-0 translate-middle এর মাধ্যমে element বসবে top-left corner এ তবে element centered হবে কারণ এখানে left এ ৫০% ‍যাবে এবং উপরে এর দিকে ৫০% ‍যাবে।
	top-100 start-100 translate-middle এর মাধ্যমে element বসবে bottom-left corner এ তবে element centered হবে কারণ এখানে left এ ৫০% ‍যাবে এবং উপরে এর দিকে ৫০% ‍যাবে।
	
	translate-middle:
		Applies CSS transformations:
		translateX(-50%): Moves the element 50% of its width to the left.
		translateY(-50%): Moves the element 50% of its height upwards.


	<div class="position-relative bg-light mt-5 bg-secondary" style="height: 300px;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
		<div class="position-absolute top-100 start-100 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
    </div>




By adding .translate-middle-x or .translate-middle-y classes, elements can be positioned only in horizontal or vertical direction.
(horizontal এবং vertically center করার জন্য element ব্যবহৃত হবে।)
	
	 <div class="position-relative bg-light mt-5" style="height: 300px;">
       
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-50 translate-middle-x  bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-50 translate-middle bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 start-50 translate-middle-x bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        
     </div>
	 
	 


<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <title>Sticky Fix</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container-md">
    <!-- Sticky Positioning -->
    <h2 class="mt-4">Sticky Positioning</h2>
    <div class="position-sticky top-0 bg-warning text-dark p-3" style="z-index: 1020;">
        <p class="mb-0">I stick to the top when scrolling!</p>
    </div>

    <!-- Static Positioning -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Static Positioning</h2>
    <div class="bg-secondary text-white p-3 mb-4">
        <p class="mb-0">This box has static positioning (default behavior).</p>
    </div>

    <!-- Relative and Absolute Positioning -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Relative and Absolute Positioning (1)</h2>
    <div class="position-relative bg-primary text-white p-4 mb-4" style="height: 150px;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0 bg-danger text-white p-2">
            I'm positioned absolutely within the relative container.
        </div>
    </div>

    <h2 class="mt-5">Relative and Absolute Positioning (2)</h2>
    <div class="position-relative bg-primary text-white p-4 mb-4" style="height: 150px;">
        <p class="mb-0">This box is <strong>relative</strong>.</p>
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 end-0 bg-danger text-white p-2">
            I'm positioned absolutely within the relative container.
        </div>
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 start-0 bg-warning text-dark p-2">
            I'm positioned at the bottom-left corner.
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Fixed Positioning -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Fixed Positioning</h2>
    <div class="position-fixed bottom-0 start-0 bg-success text-white p-3">
        <p class="mb-0">Fixed to the top-right corner of the viewport.</p>
    </div>

    <!-- Centering with Translate -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Centering with Translate</h2>
    <div class="position-relative bg-info text-white p-4" style="height: 200px;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-50 translate-middle bg-dark text-white p-3">
            Centered Element
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Multiple Elements with Offsets -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Multiple Elements with Offsets</h2>
    <div class="position-relative mt-5 bg-light" style="height: 150px;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0 bg-primary text-white p-2">
            Top-Left
        </div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 end-0 bg-danger text-white p-2">
            Top-Right
        </div>
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 start-0 bg-success text-white p-2">
            Bottom-Left
        </div>
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 end-0 bg-warning text-dark p-2">
            Bottom-Right
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Grid of Positioned Elements -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Grid of Positioned Elements</h2>
    <div class="position-relative bg-light mt-5 bg-secondary" style="height: 300px;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-50 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-100 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-0 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-50 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-100 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-100 start-0 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-100 start-50 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-100 start-100 translate-middle p-3 bg-primary">XYZ</div>
    </div>

    <!-- Nested Positioned Elements -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Nested Positioned Elements</h2>
    <div class="position-relative bg-light mt-5" style="height: 300px;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0 bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-50 translate-middle-x  bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-0 end-0 bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-0 translate-middle-y bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-50 translate-middle bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 end-0 translate-middle-y bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 start-0 bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 start-50 translate-middle-x bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
        <div class="position-absolute bottom-0 end-0 bg-danger p-3">XYZ</div>
    </div>

    <!-- Aligned Positioned Elements -->
    <h2 class="mt-5">Aligned Positioned Elements</h2>
    <div class="position-relative mt-5" style="height: 300px; width: 100%; border: 1px solid black;">
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-50 translate-middle bg-primary text-white p-3">
            Centered
        </div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 start-0 translate-middle-y bg-success text-white p-3">
            Center Left
        </div>
        <div class="position-absolute top-50 end-0 translate-middle-y bg-danger text-white p-3">
            Center Right
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Specific Corner Elements -->

        <div class="position-absolute top-0 start-0  bg-primary text-white p-3">

################################################################################################



d-none: Hides the element, making it invisible and removing it from the document flow.
(d-none দিলে element টি hidden থাকবে।)

d-inline: Makes the element behave like an inline element, allowing other elements to sit on the same line.
(d-inline দিলে block element হয়ে যাবে inline)

d-block: Converts the element to a block-level element, making it occupy the full width of its container.
(inline element হয়ে যাবে block element)

d-inline-block: Combines the characteristics of inline and block elements. The element remains inline but allows setting height and width.
(d-inline-block এর মাধ্যমে element inline হবে তবে এক্ষেত্রে inline element এর size দিতে পারব।)


(screen size এর উপর ভিত্তি করে block/none করা যাবে।)
md: 720px
screen size 768px এর উপরে গেলে display block/display-none বসবে।

d-md-block: Displays the element as a block starting from the md (medium) breakpoint and above.

d-md-none: Hides the element starting from the md (medium) breakpoint and above.





<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Display & Position</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h1 class="mb-5">Display & Position</h1>

    <!-- Display None -->
    <h2>Display None</h2>
    <p class="d-none">This text is hidden</p>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Display Inline -->
    <h2>Display Inline</h2>
    <div class="d-inline">This text is inline</div>
    <div class="d-inline">This text is inline</div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Display Block -->
    <h2>Display Block</h2>
    <span class="d-block">This span is block</span>
    <span class="d-block">This span is block</span>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Display Inline Block -->
    <h2>Display Inline Block</h2>
    <span class="d-inline-block" style="width: 500px">
        This span is inline-block
      </span>
    <span class="d-inline-block">This span is inline-block</span>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Hide on Small Screens -->
    <h2>Hide on Small Screens</h2>
    <div class="d-none d-md-block">This div is hidden on mobile</div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Hide on Medium Screens and Up -->
    <h2>Hide on Medium Screens and Up</h2>
    <div class="d-block d-md-none">
        This div is hidden on medium screens and up
    </div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Don't go past here -->
</div>

---------------------------------------------------4. Background & Text Colors-----------------------------------------------------

(Background,Text,Link color সেট করা হয়েছে।)

Background Colors
Use .bg-* for background colors:
Example: .bg-primary, .bg-success, .bg-warning, .bg-dark, etc.

Text Colors
Use .text-* for text colors:
Example: .text-primary, .text-success, .text-danger, .text-dark, etc.

Link Colors
Use .link-* for styled links:
Example: .link-primary, .link-success, .link-danger, .link-warning, etc.

Background Opacity
Use .bg-opacity-* for background transparency:
Example: .bg-opacity-75, .bg-opacity-50, .bg-opacity-25, etc.


Text Opacity
Use .text-opacity-* for text transparency:
Example: .text-opacity-75, .text-opacity-50, .text-opacity-25, etc.


Gradient Background
Use .bg-gradient with .bg-* to apply gradient effects:
Example: .bg-primary bg-gradient, .bg-info bg-gradient.

-------------------------------------------------5. Spacing (margin padding)-------------------------------------------------------

Where property is one of:( margin ও padding )

m - for set margin
p - for set padding

Where sides is one of:

t - for set margin-top or padding-top(top থেকে margin/padding হবে )
b - for set margin-bottom or padding-bottom(bottom থেকে margin/padding হবে)
s - (start) for  set margin-left or padding-left (left থেকে margin/padding হবে)
e - (end) for  set margin-right or padding-right (end থেকে margin/padding হবে)
x - for classes that set both *-left and *-right (left ও right উভয় থেকে margin/padding হবে)
y - for classes that set both *-top and *-bottom (top ও bottom উভয় থেকে margin/padding হবে)
blank - for classes that set a margin or padding on all 4 sides of the element (top থেকে margin/padding হবে)
Where size is one of:

0 - 0
1 -  .25rem
2 -  .5rem
3 -  .1rem
4 -  1.5rem
5 -    3rem
auto - for classes that set the margin to auto


margin,padding apply:
m-1/p-1 (Margin/Padding All(সব দিক(top,end,bottom,start) থেকে margin apply হবে।) 
my-1/py-1 (Margin/Padding Top & Bottom (my/py দিয়ে margin/padding => Top Bottom এ apply হবে।)
mx-1/px-1(Margin/Padding Left & Right (mx দিয়ে margin => left right এ apply হবে।))
mt-1/pt-1(Margin/Padding Top (mt/pt দিয়ে margin/padding => top এ apply হবে।))
mb-1/pb-1 (Margin/Padding Bottom (mb/pb দিয়ে margin/padding => bottom এ apply হবে।)
ms-1/ps-1(Margin/Padding Left/Start)
me-1/pe-1 (Margin/Padding right/end)

(Block/Flex Box এ margin-auto use হয়।)
m-auto: Automatically centers the element in both vertical and horizontal directions.
(Block/Flex Box এর মধ্যে content কে horizontally ও vertically center এ নিয়ে আসা যায়।)
	<div class="text-bg-warning w-50 m-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    <div class="d-flex mb-5" style="height: 200px;border: 1px solid red">
        <div class="text-bg-warning w-50 m-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    </div>
my-auto: Vertically centers the element within its parent.
(Block/Flex Box এর মধ্যে content কে  vertically center এ নিয়ে আসা যায়।)

	<div class="text-bg-primary w-50 my-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    <div class="d-flex mb-5" style="height: 200px;border: 1px solid red">
        <div class="text-bg-primary w-50 my-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    </div>	

mx-auto: Horizontally centers the element within its parent.
(Block/Flex Box এর মধ্যে content কে  horizontally center এ নিয়ে আসা যায়।)
	<div class="text-bg-info w-50 mx-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    <div class="d-flex mb-5" style="height: 200px;border: 1px solid red">
        <div class="text-bg-success w-50 mx-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    </div>
	

ms-auto: Pushes the element to the right (in LTR) by setting an automatic margin on the left side.
(Block/Flex Box এর মধ্যে content কে  right এ নিয়ে যাবে।(Right Align)))
	<div class="text-bg-danger w-50 ms-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    <div class="d-flex mb-5" style="height: 200px;border: 1px solid red">
        <div class="text-bg-danger w-50 ms-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    </div>


me-auto: Pushes the element to the left (in LTR) by setting an automatic margin on the right side.
(Block/Flex Box এর মধ্যে content কে  left এ নিয়ে যাবে।(Left Align)))

	<div class="text-bg-dark w-50 me-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    <div class="d-flex mb-5" style="height: 200px;border: 1px solid red">
        <div class="text-bg-dark w-50 me-auto">Lorem, ipsum dolor.</div>
    </div>

-------------------------------------------------------06-sizing-borders-shadows--------------------------------------------------------------------
Border Classes:
border: Adds a border to all sides.
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border">Regular</div>
	
border-{color}: Sets the border color (e.g., border-primary, border-secondary, border-success, etc.).
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border border-primary">Primary</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border border-primary-subtle">Primary Subtle</div>
	
border-{size}: Sets the border thickness (e.g., border-1, border-2, border-3, border-5).
	<div class="border border-1">Border size 1</div>
    <div class="border border-2">Border size 2</div>
	
border-{side}: Adds a border to a specific side (e.g., border-top, border-end, border-bottom, border-start).
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border-top">Border Top</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border-bottom">Border Bottom</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border-end">Border Right</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border-start">Border Left</div>
border-{side}-0: Removes the border from a specific side (e.g., border-top-0, border-end-0).
	<div class="border  bg-light  border-0 mb-1">No border</div>
    <div class="border bg-light  border-top-0 mb-1">No top border</div>
    <div class="border  bg-light border-end-0 mb-1">No right border</div>
    <div class="border bg-light  border-bottom-0 mb-1">No bottom border</div>
    <div class="border  bg-light border-start-0 mb-1">No left border</div>


Rounded Border Classes:
rounded: Adds default rounded corners to all sides.
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded">Rounded Default</div>
	
rounded-{size}: Adjusts the roundness of the corners (e.g., rounded-0, rounded-1, rounded-2, rounded-3, rounded-4, rounded-5).
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-0">Rounded 0</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-1">Rounded 1</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-2">Rounded 2</div>
	
rounded-{side}: Rounds specific sides (e.g., rounded-top, rounded-end, rounded-bottom, rounded-start).
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded">Rounded Default</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-top">Rounded Top</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-bottom">Rounded Bottom</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-end">Rounded Right</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light border rounded-start">Rounded Left</div>
	
rounded-circle: Creates a circular border.
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light w-25 border rounded-circle">Rounded Circle</div>
rounded-pill: Creates a pill-shaped border.
	<div class="p-3 mb-2 bg-light w-25 border rounded-pill">Rounded Circle</div>

Special Combined Classes:
	<div class="w-25 p-5 rounded-bottom-1 bg-primary mb-3">75*75</div>
    <div class="w-25 p-5 rounded-start-2 bg-danger mb-3">75*75</div>
    <div class="w-25 p-5 rounded-end-circle bg-info mb-3">75*75</div>
    <div class="w-25 p-5 rounded-start-circle bg-info mb-3">75*75</div>
    <div class="w-25 p-5 rounded-start-pill bg-success mb-3">75*75</div>
    <div class="w-25 p-5 rounded-top-0 rounded-5 bg-success mb-3">75*75</div>

Shadow:
    <div class="p-3 mb-5 shadow-none">No shadow</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-5 shadow-sm">Small shadow</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-5 shadow">Regular shadow</div>
    <div class="p-3 mb-5 shadow-lg">Larger shadow</div>

---------------------------------------------------------------(2.7.2) 7. Breakpoints---------------------------------------------------------

Media Queries are CSS rules that allow styles to be applied conditionally, based on the device's screen size, orientation, or resolution.
device's screen size, orientation, or resolution এর condition উপর ভিত্তি করে css apply করতে চাইলে @media(condition) ব্যবহৃত হয়।
 
If @media (min-width: 576px) is defined, the styles inside this media query will apply to screens 576px or wider.
(screen size 576px এর উপরে / সমান হলে css apply হবে।)

		/* `sm` applies to x-small devices (portrait phones, less than 576px) */
		(576px এর সমান/উপরে হলে background red হয়ে যাবে।)
        @media(min-width: 576px) {
            body{
                background: red;
            }
        }
		
		 /* `md` applies to small devices (landscape phones, less than 768px) */
		 (768px এর সমান/উপরে হলে background blue হয়ে যাবে।)
        @media (min-width: 768px) {
            body {
                background: blue;
            }
        }
        /* `lg` applies to medium devices (tablets, less than 992px) */
		 (992px এর সমান/উপরে হলে background green হয়ে যাবে।)
        @media (min-width: 992px) {
            body {
                background: green;
            }
        }
        /* `xl` applies to large devices (desktops, less than 1200px) */
		 (1200px এর সমান/উপরে হলে background yellow হয়ে যাবে।)
        @media (min-width: 1200px) {
            body {
                background: yellow;
            }
        }
        /* `xxl` applies to x-large devices (large desktops, less than 1400px) */
		 (1400px এর সমান/উপরে হলে background purple হয়ে যাবে।)
        @media (min-width: 1400px) {
            body {
                background: purple;
            }
        }
		

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <style>
        /*  X-Small devices (portrait phones, less than 576px) */
        body {
            background: gray;
        }

        /* `sm` applies to x-small devices (portrait phones, less than 576px) */
        @media(min-width: 576px) {
            body{
                background: red;
            }
        }

        /* `md` applies to small devices (landscape phones, less than 768px) */
        @media (min-width: 768px) {
            body {
                background: blue;
            }
        }
        /* `lg` applies to medium devices (tablets, less than 992px) */
        @media (min-width: 992px) {
            body {
                background: green;
            }
        }
        /* `xl` applies to large devices (desktops, less than 1200px) */

        @media (min-width: 1200px) {
            body {
                background: yellow;
            }
        }
        /* `xxl` applies to x-large devices (large desktops, less than 1400px) */
        @media (min-width: 1400px) {
            body {
                background: purple;
            }
        }
    </style>
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Breakpoints</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h1 class="mb-5">Breakpoints</h1>

    <!-- Don't go past here -->
</div>
<div style="margin-top: 350px"></div>

<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

-----------------------------------------------------(2.9) 9. Navbar , gap used here -------------------------------------------------------------------------------

https://getbootstrap.com/docs/5.3/components/navbar/
( Bootstrap এর Built-in navbar use করব।)

**************************************(navbar কখন expand হবে)******************************************************************
<!--
navbar: A Bootstrap utility class for creating a responsive navigation bar.
(navbar এর জন্য এই tag use করব।)
sticky-top: Makes the navigation bar stick to the top of the page when scrolling. It stays visible as you scroll down.
(sticky-top দিয়ে navbar উপরে থাকবে।)
navbar-expand-sm: Specifies that the navbar should be collapsed (stacked vertically) on smaller screens and expanded (horizontal layout) on screen widths small (sm) and above (≥576px).
(navbar-expand-sm দিয়ে screen size 576px এর উপরে(>=576px) হলে navbar expand হবে  576px এর নীচে হলে collapse থাকবে।)
bg-primary-subtle: Adds a subtle background color variation based on the primary theme color (available in Bootstrap 5.3+). The primary theme color is defined by your Bootstrap configuration.-->
(navbar এর background color পরিবর্তন করে দিব।)

<nav class="navbar sticky-top navbar-expand-sm bg-primary-subtle ">

********************************************(navbar full screen হবে।)************************************************************

<div class="container-fluid">
A `container-fluid` creates a full-width, responsive container that spans 100% of the viewport width.
(navbar এর width 100% হবে।)


**********************************************(navbar এ image/text show হবে।)**********************************************************

navbar-brand: A Bootstrap class used to style branding/logo links in a navbar.
(navbar এ image/text দেয়ার জন্য navbar-brand use হয়।)

mt-0: A margin utility class that sets the top margin to 0.
d-inline-block: Displays the element as an inline block (useful for aligning inline elements with some block-like behavior).

align-text-top: Aligns the image's top with the top of the text next to it.

<a class="navbar-brand" href="#">
	<img class="mt-0" src="public/image/app-store.png" alt="Logo" width="30" height="24" class="d-inline-block align-text-top">
	Bootstrap
</a>

**********************************************(button(three horizontal lines) style এখান থেকে পরিবর্তন করা যাবে। )**********************************************************
*********************( এই button দেখাবে যদি ‍screen size <576px হয় কারণ navbar-expand-sm দেয়া। এবং data-bs-toggle="collapse" দেয়ায় menu item hidden হবে। )**************************************

navbar-toggler: A Bootstrap class for styling the button used to toggle (show/hide) the navbar menu on smaller screens.

navbar-toggler-icon (inside <span>): A Bootstrap class that adds a hamburger icon (three horizontal lines) inside the toggle button.
(icon পরিবর্তন করা যাবে।)

Additional Attributes:
data-bs-toggle="collapse": Enables the toggle functionality for collapsing or expanding the targeted element.
data-bs-target="#navbarSupportedContent": Specifies the ID of the element (e.g., a collapsible menu) to toggle.
aria-controls="navbarSupportedContent": Improves accessibility by specifying the ID of the collapsible element the button controls.
aria-expanded="false": Indicates the current state of the collapsible element (false = collapsed).
aria-label="Toggle navigation": Provides an accessible label for screen readers.

		/* এটা দিয়ে তিনটা horizontal line এর color change করা যাবে। color change: stroke="rgba%28255, 255, 255, 0.8 ===>means: rgba(255,255,255,0.8) stroke-width="2" line এর width : 2*/
		 .navbar-toggler .navbar-toggler-icon {
            background-image: url('data:image/svg+xml;charset=utf8,%3Csvg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="%23ffffff" viewBox="0 0 30 30"%3E%3Cpath stroke="rgba%28255, 255, 255, 0.8%29" stroke-width="2" d="M4 7h22M4 15h22M4 23h22"/%3E%3C/svg%3E');
        }

        /* Change the background and border color of the button */
		/*button এর border color , background-color এখান থেকে পরিবর্তন করা যাবে।*/
        .navbar-toggler {
            border-color: #ffffff; /* Button border color */
            background-color: #007bff; /* Button background color */
        }


        /* Optional: Add hover styles */
        /*  যখন button এ ক্লিক করা হয় তখন  background,border-color,border-shadow তা ঠিক করা হয়।*/
		/*box shadow width 10px;*/
        .navbar-toggler:hover {
            background-color: #0056b3; /* Darker shade of blue */
            border-color: #0056b3;
            box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(179, 0, 164, 1); /* Blue shadow around the button */
            /*box-shadow: none;*/
        }
<button class="navbar-toggler" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#navbarSupportedContent" aria-controls="navbarSupportedContent" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Toggle navigation">
	<span class="navbar-toggler-icon"></span>
</button>

**********************************************( xsm(screen size <576px এর জন্য navbar-collapse item গুলো hidden থাকবে যখন ক্লিক করবে তখন menuitem show হবে।) )**********************************************************
<!--   collapse work for small screen size(<576px;)-->
<!-- Collapsible menu -->
<!--On small screens (xsm), the navbar menu is collapsed and hidden by default. Clicking the toggle button will display the menu items.
    On larger screens (sm, md, etc.), the menu is always visible.-->

        <div class="collapse navbar-collapse text-center" id="navbarSupportedContent">

 <!--  navbar কে left এ নিতে হলে  me-md-auto দিতে হবে:      <ul class="navbar-nav m-auto m-md-0 me-md-auto mb-2 mb-md-0 gap-1 gap-md-4">-->

<!--
m-auto: for Small screens (< md): <ul> place in center
m-md-0: clear all margin; Overrides the m-auto class starting from the medium (md) breakpoint (≥ 768px), removing all margins.
ms-md-auto: Applies a left align from the medium (md) breakpoint(>=768px),
ms-md-auto: Applies a left align from the medium (md) breakpoint(>=768px),
mb-2 : margin bottom for all screen size (here : for small screen(>=576px and <768px))
mb-md-0 : for md screen(>=768px) margin bottom 0
gap-1 : for all screen (here : for small screen(>=576px and <768px))
gap-md-4 : for md screen(>=768px) gap-4-->


 <ul class="navbar-nav m-auto m-md-0 ms-md-auto mb-2 mb-md-0 gap-1 gap-md-4">

 ********************************************** button **********************************************************


 <!-- Responsive Buttons -->
            <!--Class Explanation
            d-flex:

            Applies the flexbox layout to the container, making its children (e.g., buttons) flexible and aligned using flexbox rules.
            By default, this means the children are laid out horizontally.
            flex-column:

            On extra small screens (<576px), the children are stacked vertically.
            d-sm-flex:

            From small screens (≥576px) and larger, the container switches back to a flexbox layout (horizontal by default).
            flex-sm-row:

            From small screens (≥576px), the children are laid out horizontally in a row.
            mt-3 mt-sm-0:

            mt-3: Adds a top margin of 1rem (16px) to the container on extra small screens (<576px).
            mt-sm-0: Removes the top margin on small screens (≥576px) and larger.
            gap-3 gap-sm-1 gap-md-2:

            Controls the spacing (gap) between the children based on screen size:
            gap-3: On extra small screens (<576px), the gap between children is 1rem (16px).
            gap-sm-1: On small screens (≥576px), the gap between children is reduced to 0.25rem (4px).
            gap-md-2: On medium screens (≥768px), the gap between children is slightly increased to 0.5rem (8px).-->
            <div class="d-flex flex-column d-sm-flex flex-sm-row mt-3 mt-sm-0 gap-3 gap-sm-1 gap-md-2 ms-md-2">
                <button type="button" class="btn btn-primary py-sm-2 px-sm-0 px-md-4">Sign up</button>
                <button type="button" class="btn btn-danger py-sm-2 px-sm-0 px-md-4">Login</button>
            </div>

<!--navbar: A Bootstrap utility class for creating a responsive navigation bar.

        <!-- when collapse in extra small screen(<576px) than  this button showing-->

        <button class="navbar-toggler " type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#navbarSupportedContent" aria-controls="navbarSupportedContent" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Toggle navigation">
            <span class="navbar-toggler-icon"></span>
        </button>

        <!--   collapse work for small screen size(<576px;)-->
        <!-- Collapsible menu -->
        <!--On small screens (xsm), the navbar menu is collapsed and hidden by default. Clicking the toggle button will display the menu items.
        On larger screens (sm, md, etc.), the menu is always visible.-->
        <div class="collapse navbar-collapse text-center" id="navbarSupportedContent">

            <!--   for navbar in left         <ul class="navbar-nav m-auto m-md-0 me-md-auto mb-2 mb-md-0 gap-1 gap-md-4">-->

            <!-- navbar in right  write regarding to your need ; make navbar responsive-->
            <!--
            m-auto: for Small screens (< md): <ul> place in center
            m-md-0: clear all margin; Overrides the m-auto class starting from the medium (md) breakpoint (≥ 768px), removing all margins.
            ms-md-auto: Applies a left align from the medium (md) breakpoint(>=768px),
            ms-md-auto: Applies a left align from the medium (md) breakpoint(>=768px),
            mb-2 : margin bottom for all screen size (here : for small screen(>=576px and <768px))
            mb-md-0 : for md screen(>=768px) margin bottom 0
            gap-1 : for all screen (here : for small screen(>=576px and <768px))
            gap-md-4 : for md screen(>=768px) gap-4-->

            <ul class="navbar-nav m-auto m-md-0 ms-md-auto mb-2 mb-md-0 gap-1 gap-md-4">

                <li class="nav-item">
                    <a class="nav-link active" aria-current="page" href="#">Home</a>
                </li>
                <li class="nav-item">
                    <a class="nav-link" href="#">About</a>
                </li>
                <li class="nav-item">
                    <a class="nav-link" href="#">Contact</a>
                </li>
                <li class="nav-item dropdown">
                    <a class="nav-link dropdown-toggle" href="#" role="button" data-bs-toggle="dropdown" aria-expanded="false">
                        Dropdown
                    </a>
                    <ul class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-end bg-white">
                        <li><a class="dropdown-item text-dark" href="#">Action</a></li>
                        <li><a class="dropdown-item text-dark" href="#">Another action</a></li>
                        <li><hr class="dropdown-divider bg-dark"></li>
                        <li><a class="dropdown-item text-dark" href="#">Something else here</a></li>
                    </ul>
                </li>



            </ul>

            <!-- according to screen size here i make button responsive-->
            <!--<button type="button" class="btn btn-primary py-sm-2 px-sm-0  px-md-4 me-2 ms-0 ms-md-2" type="">Sign up</button>
            <button type="button" class="btn btn-danger py-sm-2 px-sm-0  px-md-4 " type="">Login</button>-->


            <!-- Responsive Buttons -->
            <!--Class Explanation
            d-flex:

            Applies the flexbox layout to the container, making its children (e.g., buttons) flexible and aligned using flexbox rules.
            By default, this means the children are laid out horizontally.
            flex-column:

            On extra small screens (<576px), the children are stacked vertically.
            d-sm-flex:

            From small screens (≥576px) and larger, the container switches back to a flexbox layout (horizontal by default).
            flex-sm-row:

            From small screens (≥576px), the children are laid out horizontally in a row.
            mt-3 mt-sm-0:

            mt-3: Adds a top margin of 1rem (16px) to the container on extra small screens (<576px).
            mt-sm-0: Removes the top margin on small screens (≥576px) and larger.
            gap-3 gap-sm-1 gap-md-2:

            Controls the spacing (gap) between the children based on screen size:
            gap-3: On extra small screens (<576px), the gap between children is 1rem (16px).
            gap-sm-1: On small screens (≥576px), the gap between children is reduced to 0.25rem (4px).
            gap-md-2: On medium screens (≥768px), the gap between children is slightly increased to 0.5rem (8px).-->
            <div class="d-flex flex-column d-sm-flex flex-sm-row mt-3 mt-sm-0 gap-3 gap-sm-1 gap-md-2 ms-md-2">
                <button type="button" class="btn btn-primary py-sm-2 px-sm-0 px-md-4">Sign up</button>
                <button type="button" class="btn btn-danger py-sm-2 px-sm-0 px-md-4">Login</button>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>
</nav>

<div class="container">

</div>




<script src="assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

-----------------------------------------------------(2.10) 10. Dark Mode & Variables -------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 data-bs-theme="dark"  দিয়ে যে কোন element/component/body এর উপর theme apply করা যাবে।
 https://getbootstrap.com/docs/5.3/customize/color-modes/#dark-mode
 
 
######################################theme apply#############################################
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport"
          content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, minimum-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css">
    <style>
        /*we can change color by own*/
        /*this color we get from bootstrap: https://getbootstrap.com/docs/5.3/customize/css-variables/#root-variables*/
        body{
            background: var( --bs-success);
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <div class="card mt-5" style="width: 500px;">
        <div class="card-header">Dark Mode Card</div>
        <div class="card-body">
            Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="card mt-5" style="width: 500px;" data-bs-theme="light">
        <div class="card-header">Light Mode Card</div>
        <div class="card-body">
            Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script src="assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>


###################################### toogle button for theme #############################################
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport"
          content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, minimum-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css">
    <style>
        /* Optional: Define additional styles for dark and light themes */
    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <button id="theme-toggle" class="btn btn-primary mt-5">Toggle Theme</button>

    <div class="card mt-5" style="width: 500px;">
        <div class="card-header">Dark Mode Card</div>
        <div class="card-body">
            Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="card mt-5" style="width: 500px;" data-bs-theme="light">
        <div class="card-header">Light Mode Card</div>
        <div class="card-body">
            Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy Utsab Roy
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script>
    const toggleButton = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
    const body = document.body;

    toggleButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const currentTheme = body.getAttribute('data-bs-theme');
        const newTheme = currentTheme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';
        body.setAttribute('data-bs-theme', newTheme);
    });
</script>
<script src="assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>








==============================================================================3. Bootstrap Fundamentals - Part Two===============================================================================================

----------------------------------------------------------------------------(3.1) 1. Bootstrap Grid & Columns (gutter/gap/g-)--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Container: The grid system is contained within a <div class="container"> or <div class="container-fluid">.
		   It wraps your rows and columns.

Rows and Columns: Inside the container, you create rows (<div class="row">), and within those rows, you create columns (<div class="col">). 
                  Columns are where your content goes.


Extra Small (XS)			col-	 			None (default for all devices)				for extra small devices (portrait phones)
Small (SM)					col-sm-	 			≥ 576px										for small devices (landscape phones)
Medium (MD)					col-md-	 			≥ 768px										for medium devices (tablets)
Large (LG)					col-lg-	 			≥ 992px										for large devices (desktops)
Extra Large (XL)			col-xl-	 			≥ 1200px									for extra large devices (large desktops)
XXL							col-xxl- 			≥ 1400px									for exxtra extra large devices (large desktops)


1. col: শুধু col available space equally distributed হবে।
(সমস্যা: item গুলো ছোট হয়ে যাবে কিন্তু column সংখ্যা একই থাকবে।)
		<h1 class="mb-5">If you don’t define a column width, columns will share the available space equally.</h1>
        <div class="row bg-success">
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border p-2">1 of 2</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark  border p-2">2 of 2</div>
        </div>



2.col-size:You can specify how many of these 12 columns a single element should take up.
        (Bootsrap এ Total 12 column; কোন div কত col নিবে তা col-size(col-6) দিয়ে specify করে দিতে পারি।)
		<div class="row bg-success">
            <div class="col-6 bg-light text-dark border p-2">1 of 2</div>
            <div class="col-6 bg-light text-dark  border p-2">2 of 2</div>
        </div>
		

3. col-screen size-size:(কোন screen এ div গুলো কত column নিবে /একটা row তে কতগুলো div দেখাবে তা ‍specify করা যায়।)

			<div class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3  col-xl-2   bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3">
              
            </div>
			
			col-12(মূলত সবার জন্য এটা।):(extra small screen(<576px এর জন্য 12 column নিবে div টি।))
			This specifies that the column will take up all 12 grid columns (full width) on extra small screens (less than 576px).

			col-sm-6:(small screen(>=576px এর জন্য 6 column নিবে div টি।।))
			On small screens (≥576px), the column will take up 6 grid columns (half the width).

			col-md-4:(medium screen(≥768px এর জন্য 4 column নিবে div টি।))
			On medium screens (≥768px), the column will take up 4 grid columns (one-third of the row width).

			col-lg-3:(large screen(<576px এর জন্য 3 column নিবে div টি।))
			On large screens (≥992px), the column will take up 3 grid columns (one-quarter of the row width).

			col-xl-2:(extra-large screen(≥1200px এর জন্য 2 column নিবে div টি।))
			On extra-large screens (≥1200px), the column will take up 2 grid columns (one-sixth of the row width)
			

4. row-cols-number :  Use the responsive .row-cols-* classes to quickly set the number of columns
                      (এর মাধ্যেমে দ্রুত একটা div গুলো column নিতে তা ‍specify করা যায়।)
					  (এখানে প্রতি row তে দুটি column থাকবে(col-6 করে নিবে প্রতি div)।)
			<div class="row row-cols-2">
				<div class=" col  bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3">
					1 of 7
				</div>
			</div>
			
			(চাইলে screen size ও ‍specify করে দিতে পারি।)
			<div class="row row-cols-1 row-cols-sm-2  row-cols-md-3  row-cols-lg-4  row-cols-xxl-5" >


5.nesting: columnn এর ভিতরে row দিতে পারি।
		<div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-3 bg-danger p-4">
                <div class="col-8 col-sm-6 border border-success-subtle text-center py-3"> Level 2: .col-8 .col-sm-6</div>
                <div class="col-4 col-sm-6 border border-success-subtle text-center py-3"> Level 2: .col-4 .col-sm-6</div>
            </div>
            <div class="col-sm-9 bg-success py-4">
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-8 col-sm-6 border border-success-subtle text-center py-3"> Level 2: .col-8 .col-sm-6</div>
                    <div class="col-4 col-sm-6 border border-success-subtle text-center py-3"> Level 2: .col-4 .col-sm-6</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>



6.	g-size:column গুলোর মধ্যে space তৈরি করবে, row গুলোর মধ্যে space তৈরি করবে

	gx-size:column গুলোর মধ্যে space তৈরি করবে

	gy-size:row গুলোর মধ্যে space তৈরি করবে
	
	

7. Offset is used to add empty space (or margin) to the left of a column, effectively shifting it horizontally
(Offset দিয়ে left থেকে space তৈরি করবে এর ফলে div shift হয়ে right এ যাবে।)

		
		এখানে extra-small-screen এ left-margin-0
		এখানে small-screen এ left-margin-2
		এখানে medium-screen এ left-margin-3
		এখানে large-screen এ left-margin-4
		এখানে extra-large-screen এ left-margin-5
		এখানে extra-extra-small-screen এ left-margin-6
		
		<div class="row">
            <div class="col-6 offset-0 offset-sm-2 offset-md-3 offset-lg-4 offset-xl-5 offset-xxl-6 bg-light text-dark border p-3 text-center">Shift Me</div>
        </div>


8.order: order দিয়ে চাইলে ডাটাবেস থেকে dynamically col/div গুলো যে কোন order এ বসাতে পারব।
		<div class="row">
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3 order-2">Column 1</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3 order-4">Column 2</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3 order-1">Column 3</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3r order-3">Column 4</div>
        </div>




###################################################code###########################################

    <div class="container-fluid border border-1 border-danger">

        <!-- Nesting: we can put row inside col-->
        <h1 class="mb-5 mt-5">Nesting(Example 1)</h1>
        <!-- Parent Row -->
        <div class="row">
            <!-- First Main Column -->
            <div class="col-12 col-md-6 bg-light text-dark p-3 border">
                <h5>Main Column 1</h5>
                <p>This is the first main column with a nested row inside:</p>

                <!-- Nested Row -->
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-6 border border-success text-center py-2">Nested Col 1</div>
                    <div class="col-6 border border-success text-center py-2">Nested Col 2</div>
                    <div class="col-6 border border-success text-center py-2">Nested Col 3</div>
                    <div class="col-6 border border-success text-center py-2">Nested Col 4</div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Second Main Column -->
            <div class="col-12 col-md-6 bg-light text-dark p-3 border">
                <h5>Main Column 2</h5>
                <p>This is the second main column with a nested row inside:</p>

                <!-- Nested Row -->
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-4 border border-primary text-center py-2">Nested Col 1</div>
                    <div class="col-8 border border-primary text-center py-2">Nested Col 2</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>


        <!-- Nesting: we can put row inside col-->
        <h1 class="mb-5 mt-5">Nesting(Example 2)</h1>
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-sm-3 bg-danger p-4">
                Level 1: .col-sm-3
            </div>
            <div class="col-sm-9 bg-success py-4">
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-8 col-sm-6 border border-success-subtle text-center py-3"> Level 2: .col-8 .col-sm-6</div>
                    <div class="col-4 col-sm-6 border border-success-subtle text-center py-3"> Level 2: .col-4 .col-sm-6</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>


        <!--Gutter is the space (margin or padding) between columns in the grid system.
        Gutters are used to control the spacing between columns and rows to ensure a clean and structured layout.-->
        <h1 class="mb-5 mt-5">Gutter (make column space and row space)</h1>
        <div class="row g-5">
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
        </div>


        <h1 class="mb-5 mt-5">gx(gx-4: make column space) gy (g-2: make row space)</h1>
        <div class="row gx-4 gy-2">
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
            <div class=" col-md-4">
                <div class="bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3"> 1 of 4</div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- In Bootstrap, an offset is used to add empty space (or margin) to the left of a column, effectively shifting it horizontally-->
        <h1 class="mb-5 mt-5">offset is used to add empty space in left</h1>
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col-6 offset-0 offset-sm-2 offset-md-3 offset-lg-4 offset-xl-5 offset-xxl-6 bg-light text-dark border p-3 text-center">Shift Me</div>
        </div>


        <!-- Ordering -->
        <h1 class="mb-5 mt-5">Ordering</h1>
        <div class="row">
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3 order-2">Column 1</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3 order-4">Column 2</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3 order-1">Column 3</div>
            <div class="col bg-light text-dark border px-5 py-3r order-3">Column 4</div>
        </div>




    </div>

----------------------------------------------------------------------------(3.1) 2. Flexbox Classes--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

.d-flex: (which is a block-level flex container and takes up the full width of its parent)(block level container যা parent এর full width নিবে।)

	Purpose: This class applies display: flex to an element, turning it into a flex container.

	Behavior: The element becomes a block-level flex container, 
	meaning it will take up the full width of its parent by default, 
	and its children (flex items) will be laid out according to the flexbox rules.

	Use Case: Use .d-flex when you want to create a flex container that behaves like a block-level element.
	(d-flex দিয়ে element/div কে ব্লক লেভেল(পুরো row জায়গা নিবে) এ নেয়া হয় তবে এটা ‍parent এর full width নিবে।)

		***এখানে d-flex-container , parent col-md-12 কে inherit করবে এবং পুরো width(col-12) নিয়ে নিবে।
		The .d-flex container inherits the width of its parent (.col-md-12), 
		so it will take up the full 12-column width.

		***এখানে d-flex-container এর child গুলো equal space নিবে content অনুযায়ী। সম্পূর্ণ free space নিতে চাইলে flex-grow/flex-fill use করতে হয়।
		The flex items inside the .d-flex container will not automatically take up equal space 
		unless you use additional flex utilities like .flex-grow-1 or .flex-fill.
		
		<div class="col-md-12">   
			<div class="d-flex p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
				<div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
				<div class="p-3 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
				<div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
			</div>
		</div>
	
	

.d-inline-flex:. only takes up as much space as its content requires.(block level container না এটা যতটুকু content ততটুকু space নিবে।)

	Purpose: This class applies display: inline-flex to an element, turning it into an inline-level flex container.
	(d-inline-flex দিয়ে element/div কে inline বানানো যাবে। যতটুকু কনটেন্ট ততটুকু spce নিবে div টি।)
	
	Use Case: Use .d-inline-flex when you want a flex container that behaves like an inline element (e.g., for buttons, icons, or other inline components).
			
			<div class="col-md-12">   
				<div class="d-inline-flex p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>
			</div>


flex-row: Aligns flex items horizontally in the normal direction (left to right).

flex-row-reverse: Aligns flex items horizontally in the reverse direction (right to left).

flex-col: Aligns flex items vertically in the normal direction (top to bottom).

flex-col-reverse: Aligns flex items vertically in the reverse direction (bottom to top).

খুবই গুরুত্বপূর্ণ:
flex-row তে main axis->Left to Right, cross axis->top to bottom
flex-row (default):
Main Axis: Horizontal (left to right)
Cross Axis: Vertical (top to bottom)

flex-column তে main axis->top to bottom, cross axis->left to right
flex-column:
Main Axis: Vertical (top to bottom)
Cross Axis: Horizontal (left to right)

+++++++++++++++++++justify-content কাজ করে Main Axis এ+++++++++++++++++++++++
flex-row এর জন্য justify-content:(Main Axis: Horizontal (left to right))
.justify-content-start: Aligns items to the start of the main axis.(Horizontal Row এর left এ থাকবে)

.justify-content-end: Aligns items to the end of the main axis.(Horizontal Row এর right এ থাকবে)

.justify-content-center: Aligns items at the center of the main axis.(Horizontal Row এর center এ থাকবে)

.justify-content-between: Distributes items evenly, with the first item at the start and the last item at the end.(Horizontal Row এর left এ first item , right এ last item থাকবে।)

.justify-content-around: Distributes items evenly with equal space around them.(Horizontal Row এর left এ ফাকা থাকবে এরপর first item , right এ ফাকা থাকবে এরপর last item থাকবে।)

.justify-content-evenly: Distributes items evenly with equal space between and around them.




flex-col এর জন্য justify-content: Main Axis: Vertical (top to bottom)
.justify-content-start: Aligns items to the start of the main axis.( Vertical column এর top এ থাকবে)

.justify-content-end: Aligns items to the end of the main axis.(Vertical column এর bottom এ থাকবে)

.justify-content-center: Aligns items at the center of the main axis.(Vertical column এর center এ থাকবে)

.justify-content-between: Distributes items evenly, with the first item at the start and the last item at the end.(Vertical column এর top এ first item , bottom এ last item থাকবে।)

.justify-content-around: Distributes items evenly with equal space around them.Vertical column এর top এ ফাকা থাকবে এরপর first item , bottom এ ফাকা থাকবে এরপর last item থাকবে।)

.justify-content-evenly: Distributes items evenly with equal space between and around them.




++++++++++++++++++align-itmes কাজ করে Cross Axis এ+++++++++++++++++++++
খুবই গুরুত্বপূর্ণ:

flex-row এর জন্য align-items:(Cross Axis: vertical (top to bottom))
1.flex-row:
Main Axis: Horizontal (left to right).
Cross Axis: Vertical (top to bottom).
align-items: Controls the vertical alignment of flex items.(flex row তে ‍align-items কাজ করে vertically/cross axis এ)

flex-col এর জন্য align-items:(Cross Axis: horizontal (left to right))
2..flex-col:
Main Axis: Vertical (top to bottom).
Cross Axis: Horizontal (left to right).
align-items: Controls the horizontal alignment of flex items.(flex col তে ‍align-items কাজ করে horizontally/cross axis এ)






for flex-row, align-items:
align-items-start: Aligns items to the top of the container.( Vertical column এর top এ থাকবে)

align-items-end: Aligns items to the bottom of the container.(Vertical column এর bottom এ থাকবে)

align-items-center: Centers items vertically.(Vertical column এর center এ থাকবে)

align-items-baseline: Aligns items to their baselines.

align-items-stretch: Stretches items to fill the container vertically.(div/element সম্পূর্ণ জায়গা নিয়ে নিবে vertically)



for flex-col, align-items:
align-items-start: Aligns items to the left of the container.(Horizontal Row এর left এ থাকবে)

align-items-end: Aligns items to the right of the container.(Horizontal Row এর right এ থাকবে)

align-items-center: Centers items horizontally.(Horizontal Row এর center এ থাকবে)

align-items-baseline: Not commonly used in .flex-col (works on text baselines).

align-items-stretch: Stretches items to fill the container horizontally.(div/element সম্পূর্ণ জায়গা নিয়ে নিবে horizontally)


Flex Direction	  Main Axis			     Cross Axis			   align-items Controls
.flex-row		 Horizontal				 Vertical			   Vertical alignment
.flex-col	     Vertical				 Horizontal			   Horizontal alignment






++++++++++++++++align-self ও cross direction এ কাজ করে,তবে এক্ষেত্রে single item এর উপর এটা ব্যবহার করা যায়+++++++++++++++
The align-self utility in Bootstrap is used to individually align a flex item along the cross axis,

flex-row এর জন্য:
align-self-start: Aligns the item to the top.

align-self-center: Centers the item vertically.

align-self-end: Aligns the item to the bottom.


flex-col এর জন্য:
align-self-start: Aligns the item to the left.

align-self-center: Centers the item horizontally.

align-self-end: Aligns the item to the right.



<div class="d-flex flex-row bg-secondary p-3" style="height: 150px;">
  <div class="p-2 bg-info align-self-start">Top</div>
  <div class="p-2 bg-danger align-self-center">Middle</div>
  <div class="p-2 bg-primary align-self-end">Bottom</div>
  <div class="p-2 bg-warning align-self-stretch">Stretch</div>
</div>

The first item is aligned to the top.

The second item is centered vertically.

The third item is aligned to the bottom.

The fourth item stretches to fill the height of the container.


<div class="d-flex flex-column bg-secondary p-3" style="height: 300px;">
  <div class="p-2 bg-info align-self-start">Start</div>
  <div class="p-2 bg-danger align-self-center">Center</div>
  <div class="p-2 bg-primary align-self-end">End</div>
</div>

align-self-start: Aligns the item to the top.

align-self-center: Centers the item vertically.

align-self-end: Aligns the item to the bottom.


++++++++++++++++flex-fill কাজ করে main axis এ +++++++++++++++
The flex item will expand to fill the remaining space in the container.
( সম্পূর্ণ avialable space  div দ্বারা allocate করা যায়।)

for: flex-row
<div class="d-flex">
  <div class="p-3 bg-info">Fixed Width</div>
  <div class="p-3 bg-danger flex-fill">Fill Remaining Space</div>
  <div class="p-3 bg-primary">Fixed Width</div>
</div>

The middle item (.flex-fill) will expand to fill the remaining space, while the other items retain their fixed width.


<div class="d-flex">
  <div class="p-3 bg-info flex-fill">Item 1</div>
  <div class="p-3 bg-danger flex-fill">Item 2</div>
  <div class="p-3 bg-primary flex-fill">Item 3</div>
</div>

Each item will take up equal space within the container.



for: flex-col
<div class="d-flex flex-column" style="height: 200px;">
  <div class="p-3 bg-info flex-fill">Item 1</div>
  <div class="p-3 bg-danger flex-fill">Item 2</div>
  <div class="p-3 bg-primary flex-fill">Item 3</div>
</div>

In a vertical flex container (.flex-column), .flex-fill makes each item take up equal height.




++++++++++++++++flex-grow: flex-fill: +++++++++++++++
flex-grow: Use when you want an item to expand and fill available space.
.flex-grow-0: Prevents the item from growing.

.flex-grow-1: Allows the item to grow.(item টি available space পর‌্যন্ত grow করবে।)

flex-shrink:(shrink-0 মানে item shrink হবে না।)

Purpose: Controls how much a flex item can shrink if there is not enough space in the container.

flex-shrink-0: Prevents the item from shrinking.

.flex-shrink-1: Allows the item to shrink (default behavior).


++++++++flex-wrap , flex-nowrap++++++
flex-wrap: default
flex-nowrap: wrap হবে না/নতুন লাইন যাবে সব একটা row তে।

                <h1>align-items-center: Aligns items at the center of the cross axis.</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-center p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height:300px">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>


                <!-- align-items-end: Aligns items at the end of the cross axis.-->
                <h1>align-items-end: Aligns items at the end of the cross axis.</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-end p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height:300px">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>


                <!-- align-items-stretch: Stretches items to fill the cross axis (default).-->
                <h1>align-items-stretch: Stretches items to fill the cross axis (default).</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-stretch p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height:300px">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>




                <!-- Align Self Utilities -->
                <!-- Override the cross-axis(Y-axis) alignment for specific items:-->
                <!-- align-self-start: Aligns items at the start of the cross axis.-->
                <h1>align-self-start: Aligns items at the start(top) of the cross axis(Y-axis).</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-stretch p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height: 400px;">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info align-self-start">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>

                <!-- align-self-center: Aligns  single items at the center of the cross axis.-->
                <h1>align-self-center: Aligns items at the start(top) of the cross axis(Y-axis).</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-start p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height: 400px;">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger align-self-center">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>

                <!-- align-self-end: Aligns  single items at the end of the cross axis.-->
                <h1>align-self-end: Aligns items at the end(bottom) of the cross axis(Y-axis).</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-start p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height: 400px;">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger ">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary align-self-end">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>

                <!-- align-self-stretch:  single items streetch d of the cross axis.-->
                <h1>align-self-stretch: Aligns items stretch of the cross axis(Y-axis).</h1>
                <div class="d-flex align-items-start p-3 bg-secondary text-white" style="height: 400px;">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger align-self-stretch">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary ">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>


               <!-- To use flex-fill, ensure the parent element has the d-flex class
                 then apply flex-fill to the child elements you want to stretch.-->
                <!--Item one take width according to content
                Item three take width according to content
                Item two and four take remaining space-->
                <h1>flex-fill take available space</h1>
                <div class="d-flex p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info ">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger flex-fill">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-success flex-fill">My Flex Item Four</div>
                </div>

                <hr>


                <!--    space distributed among those children -->
                <h1>d-flex take depend on content</h1>
                <div class="d-flex p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info flex-fill">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-danger flex-fill">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 bg-primary flex-fill">My Flex Item Three</div>
                </div>

                <hr>

               <!-- Wrapping Utilities
                Control whether items wrap or not:

                flex-wrap: Items wrap to the next line (default).
                flex-nowrap: Items stay in a single line.
                flex-wrap-reverse: Items wrap in reverse.-->
                <h1>flex-wrap : wrapping into next line</h1>
                <div class="d-flex flex-nowrap p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
                    <div class="p-3 col-6 bg-info ">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3 col-6 bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3 col-3 bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                    <div class="p-3 col-3 bg-success">My Flex Item Four</div>
                </div>

                <hr>


                <!-- Grow and shrink 
                Control how items grow or shrink using:
                Grow: like as flex-fill
                flex-grow-0: Disable growing.
                flex-grow-1: Enable growing.
                flex item one : take available space
                flex item two,three,four : take  space as content
               -->
                <h1> flex item one : take available space</h1>
                <div class="d-flex p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info flex-grow-1">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3  bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                    <div class="p-3  bg-primary">My Flex Item Three</div>
                    <div class="p-3  bg-success">My Flex Item Four</div>
                </div>

                <hr>
                

                <!--Use .flex-shrink-* utilities to toggle a flex item’s ability to shrink if necessary.
                In the example below, the second flex item with .flex-shrink-1 is forced to wrap its contents
                to a new line, “shrinking” to allow more space for the previous flex item with .w-100.-->

                <!--flex-shrink-0: Disable shrinking.
                flex-shrink-1: Enable shrinking.-->
                <h1> flex item two : try to shrink for giving space to item one</h1>
                <div class="d-flex p-3 bg-secondary text-white">
                    <div class="p-3 bg-info w-100">My Flex Item One</div>
                    <div class="p-3  bg-danger">My Flex Item Two</div>
                </div>

                <hr>

            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
