----------------------------------------------------------------------------(3.3) 3. Cards--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

card
	Purpose: The main container for a card.

	Usage: Wraps all card content.
	
	<div class="card">
		<!-- Card content goes here -->
	</div>

card-body
	Purpose: The main content area of the card. It typically contains text, titles, subtitles, links, etc.

	Usage: Place inside the .card to structure the main content.
	
	<div class="card">
		<div class="card-body">
			<h5 class="card-title">Title</h5>
			<p class="card-text">Some text here.</p>
		</div>
	</div>

card-title
	Purpose: Used for the title of the card.

	Usage: Typically placed inside .card-body.
	
	<div class="card-body">
		<h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
	</div>

card-subtitle
	Purpose: Used for the subtitle of the card.

	Usage: Typically placed inside .card-body, below the .card-title.
	
	<div class="card-body">
		<h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
	</div>

card-text
	Purpose: Used for the main text content of the card.

	Usage: Typically placed inside .card-body.
	
	<div class="card-body">
		<p class="card-text">This is the main content of the card.</p>
	</div>

card-link
	Purpose: Used for links inside the card.

	Usage: Typically placed inside .card-body.
	
	<div class="card-body">
		<a href="#" class="card-link">Link 1</a>
		<a href="#" class="card-link">Link 2</a>
	</div>

card-img-top
	Purpose: Places an image at the top of the card.

	Usage: Place directly inside .card, above .card-body.
	
	<div class="card">
		<img src="image.jpg" class="card-img-top" alt="Image">
		<div class="card-body">
			<h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
			<p class="card-text">Some text here.</p>
		</div>
	</div>


card-img-bottom
	Purpose: Places an image at the bottom of the card.

	Usage: Place directly inside .card, below .card-body.
	
	<div class="card">
		<div class="card-body">
			<h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
			<p class="card-text">Some text here.</p>
		</div>
		<img src="image.jpg" class="card-img-bottom" alt="Image">
	</div>

card-header
	Purpose: Adds a header section to the card.

	Usage: Place directly inside .card, above .card-body.
	
	<div class="card">
		<div class="card-header">
			Featured
		</div>
		<div class="card-body">
			<h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
			<p class="card-text">Some text here.</p>
		</div>
	</div>


card-footer
	Purpose: Adds a footer section to the card.

	Usage: Place directly inside .card, below .card-body.
	
	<div class="card">
		<div class="card-body">
			<h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
			<p class="card-text">Some text here.</p>
		</div>
		<div class="card-footer">
			Footer Content
		</div>
	</div>

card-group
	Equal Height and Width:
		(সকল card এর width,height একই থাকবে। কোন gutter/gap থাকবে না card এর মধ্যে।)
		All cards in the group will have the same height and width.

		This ensures a consistent and visually appealing layout.

	No Gutter (Spacing) Between Cards:

		By default, there is no spacing between cards in a group.

		If you want spacing, you can use .card-deck or .row with .col.

	Responsive Behavior:
		On smaller screens, the cards will stack vertically.
	
	(col এর সাইজ দিয়ে কোন কাজ হবে না।)
	div class="row">
        <div class="col">
            <div class="card-group">
                <div class="card">
                    <img src="public/image/background.jpg" class="card-img-top" alt="...">
                    <div class="card-body">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Card title</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This is a wider card with supporting text below as a natural lead-in to
                            additional
                            content. This content is a little bit longer.</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="card-footer">
                        <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="card">
                    <img src="public/image/environment.webp" class="card-img-top" alt="...">
                    <div class="card-body">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Card title</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This card has supporting text below as a natural lead-in to additional
                            content.</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="card-footer">
                        <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="card">
                    <img src="public/image/background.jpg" class="card-img-top" alt="...">
                    <div class="card-body">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Card title</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This is a wider card with supporting text below as a natural lead-in to
                            additional
                            content. This card has even longer content than the first to show that equal height
                            action.</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="card-footer">
                        <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>


Card Grid Layout
row-cols-1 row-cols-md-2 g-4
	row-cols-2 মানে একটা row তে ২ টা column থাকবে।
	এজন্য col এর size দিতে হবে না।
	<div class="row row-cols-1 row-cols-md-2 g-4">
        <!--for row-col-2 we mention how many grid we can place.
        so, we don't need to mention col-size-->
        <div class="col">
            <div class="card">
                <img src="public/image/background.jpg" class="card-img-top" alt="...">
                <div class="card-body">
                    <h5 class="card-title">Card title</h5>
                    <p class="card-text">This is a longer card with supporting text below as a natural lead-in to
                        additional content. This content is a little bit longer.</p>
                </div>
                <div class="card-footer">
                    <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="col">
            <div class="card">
                <img src="public/image/desk.avif" class="card-img-top" alt="...">
                <div class="card-body">
                    <h5 class="card-title">Card title</h5>
                    <p class="card-text">This is a longer card with supporting text below as a natural lead-in to
                        additional content. This content is a little bit longer.</p>
                </div>
                <div class="card-footer">
                    <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
	</div>
	
	
Card Grid Layout(All card & picture same size)
	
	এখানে card এর size সবার সমান = h-100 এবং  picture এর size একই করা হয়েছে। 


Card Navigation with tab
	 Card Structure:
		<div class="card text-center">
		This creates a Bootstrap card with centered text.
	Card Header with Tabs:
		<div class="card-header">
			<ul class="nav nav-tabs card-header-tabs" id="myTab" role="tablist">
		
		The .card-header contains the tab navigation.

		The .nav and .nav-tabs classes create a tabbed navigation bar.

		The id="myTab" is used to associate the tabs with their content.
	
	Tab Buttons:
		<li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
			<button class="nav-link active" id="tab-1" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#tab1-content" type="button" role="tab" aria-controls="tab1-content" aria-selected="true">Tab 1</button>
		</li>
		
		Each <li> represents a tab button.

		The class="nav-link" makes the button look like a tab.

		The data-bs-toggle="tab" attribute enables the tab functionality.

		The data-bs-target="#tab1-content" links the button to the corresponding content panel.

		The aria-controls="tab1-content" and aria-selected="true" are for accessibility.
		
	Tab Content Panels:
		<div class="card-body tab-content">
			<div class="tab-pane fade show active" id="tab1-content" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-1">
				<h5 class="card-title">Tab 1 Content</h5>
				<p class="card-text">This is content for Tab 1.</p>
			</div>
		The .tab-content container holds all the tab panels.

		Each .tab-pane represents the content for a specific tab.

		The id="tab1-content" matches the data-bs-target of the corresponding tab button.

		The fade class adds a smooth fade transition when switching tabs.

		The show active class makes this tab visible by default.
		
	<div class="row">
        <div class="col-12">
            <div class="card text-center mb-5">
                <div class="card-header">
                    <ul class="nav nav-tabs card-header-tabs" id="myTab" role="tablist">
                        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
                            <button class="nav-link active" id="tab-1" data-bs-toggle="tab"
                                    data-bs-target="#tab1-content"
                                    type="button" role="tab" aria-controls="tab1-content" aria-selected="true">Tab 1
                            </button>
                        </li>
                        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
                            <button class="nav-link" id="tab-2" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#tab2-content"
                                    type="button" role="tab" aria-controls="tab2-content" aria-selected="false">Tab 2
                            </button>
                        </li>
                        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
                            <button class="nav-link" id="tab-3" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#tab3-content"
                                    type="button" role="tab" aria-controls="tab3-content" aria-selected="false">Tab 3
                            </button>
                        </li>
                    </ul>
                </div>

                <div class="card-body tab-content">
                    <div class="tab-pane fade show active" id="tab1-content" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-1">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Tab 1 Content</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This is content for Tab 1.</p>
                        <a href="#" class="btn btn-primary">Go somewhere1</a>
                    </div>
                    <div class="tab-pane fade" id="tab2-content" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-2">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Tab 2 Content</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This is content for Tab 2.</p>
                        <a href="#" class="btn btn-primary">Go somewher2</a>
                    </div>
                    <div class="tab-pane fade" id="tab3-content" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab-3">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Tab 3 Content</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This is content for Tab 3.</p>
                        <a href="#" class="btn btn-primary">Go somewher3</a>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

        .fixed-image-height {
            height: 200px; /* Set a fixed height for all images */
            object-fit: cover; /* Ensures the image covers the area without distortion */
            width: 100%; /* Ensures the image stretches to the full width of the card */
        }
    </style>

    </style>

<div class="container">
    <!--
    Basic Card Structure:
    card is block level element
     A card is created using the .card class.
     Inside the card, you can use .card-body for the main content.-->

    <!--.card-body. Use it whenever you need a padded section within a card.-->

    <h1 class="mt-3 text-bg-light"> Basic Card Structure</h1>

        <div class="col-md-3">
            <div class="card">

                    Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet,
                    consectetur adipisicing elit.
                    Aliquam cum deleniti excepturi facilis fugit
                    magnam modi, odio officia tenetur voluptates?
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>


    <!--Card Titles, Text, and Links
    Use .card-title for titles and .card-text for text content.

    Links can be styled with .card-link.-->
    <!--.card-body. Use it whenever you need a padded section within a card.-->
    <h1 class="mt-3 text-bg-light"> Card Titles, Text, and Links </h1>
    <div class="row">
        <div class="col-md-3">
            <div class="card">
                <div class="card-body">
                    <h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
                    <h6 class="card-subtitle mb-2 text-body-secondary">Card subtitle</h6>
                    <p class="card-text">Some example text for the card.Some example text for the card.</p>
                    <a href="#" class="card-link">Card Link</a>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <!--Card Images
    Add images to cards using .card-img-top or .card-img-bottom. .card-img-top-->

    <!--.card-body. Use it whenever you need a padded section within a card.-->
    <h1 class="mt-3 text-bg-light"> Add images to cards using .card-img-bottom. .card-img-top</h1>
    <div class="row">
        <div class="col-md-3">
            <div class="card">
                <img src="public/image/background.jpg" class="card-img-top" alt="No Image">
                <div class="card-body">
                    <p>Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Blanditiis commodi delectus
                        error fuga incidunt laudantium maiores praesentium quisquam veniam voluptatem!</p>
                </div>
                <img src="public/image/environment.webp" class="card-img-bottom" alt="No Image">
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <!-- Use .card-header and .card-footer for headers and footers.-->
    <!-- Header & Footer -->
    <h1 class="mt-3 text-bg-light">Use .card-header and .card-footer for headers and footers.</h1>
    <div class="row">
        <div class="col-md-3">
            <div class="card">
                <div class="card-header">Card Header</div>
                <div class="card-body">
                    <h5 class="card-title">Card Title</h5>
                    <p class="card-text">
                        Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit.
                        Repudiandae, molestias dolor minus architecto vel nemo laboriosam
                        aut temporibus ratione optio.
                    </p>
                </div>
                <div class="card-footer">Card Footer</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>


    <!-- Cards can be grouped together using-->
    <!-- .card-group is designed to display cards in a single row with equal height and width. It does not work well with .col-*-->
    <!-- Card Layouts -->
    <h1 class="mt-3 text-bg-light">Use .card-group for grouping Card</h1>
    <div class="row">
        <div class="col">
            <div class="card-group">
                <div class="card">
                    <img src="public/image/background.jpg" class="card-img-top" alt="...">

                    </div>

                        <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="card">
                    <img src="public/image/environment.webp" class="card-img-top" alt="...">
                    <div class="card-body">
                        <h5 class="card-title">Card title</h5>
                        <p class="card-text">This card has supporting text below as a natural lead-in to additional
                            content.</p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="card-footer">
                        <small class="text-body-secondary">Last updated 3 mins ago</small>
                    </div>

----------------------------------------------------------------------------(3.4) 4. List Groups & Badges --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
(list-group তৈরি করা যায় item গুলোর।)
.list-group
	Applied to the container (e.g., <ul> or <div>) to create a list group.

	Styles the container to display a list of items with borders, padding, and spacing.
	
	<ul class="list-group">
	  <li class="list-group-item">Item 1</li>
	  <li class="list-group-item">Item 2</li>
	</ul>

.list-group-item
	Applied to individual list items (e.g., <li> or <div>).

	Styles each item with padding, borders, and hover effects.
	
	<li class="list-group-item">Item 1</li>

.list-group-flush(borders and rounded corners দূর করা যায়।)
	Removes borders and rounded corners from the list group, making it flush with its container.
	
	<ul class="list-group list-group-flush">
	  <li class="list-group-item">Item 1</li>
	  <li class="list-group-item">Item 2</li>
	</ul>

.list-group-horizontal(list-group এর item গুলো horizontally করা যায়।)
	Displays list items horizontally instead of vertically.
	
	<ul class="list-group list-group-horizontal">
	  <li class="list-group-item">Item 1</li>
	  <li class="list-group-item">Item 2</li>
	</ul>

.list-group-item-action(list-group এর item হিসেবে link add করা যায়।)
	Makes list items clickable (e.g., for links or buttons).

	Adds hover and active states.
	<a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">Clickable Item</a>



Badge Classes

.badge
	Base class for creating badges.

	Styles the element as a small, rounded label.
	
	<span class="badge bg-primary">New</span>
	
.bg-*
	Adds background colors to badges.

	Examples: .bg-primary, .bg-success, .bg-danger.
	
	<span class="badge bg-success">Success</span>


.rounded-pill
	Makes the badge more rounded (pill-shaped).
	<span class="badge rounded-pill bg-warning">Warning</span>

.text-*
	Changes the text color of the badge for better contrast.

	Example: .text-white.
	
	<span class="badge bg-dark text-white">Dark</span>

<!doctype html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport"
          content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, minimum-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css">
    <style>
        .fixed-image-height {
            height: 200px; /* Set a fixed height for all images */
            object-fit: cover; /* Ensures the image covers the area without distortion */
            width: 100%; /* Ensures the image stretches to the full width of the card */
        }
    </style>
    <style>

    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <!--
    ( un-order list এর item )
    list group is an unordered list.
    -->
    <h1 class="mt-2">Make un-order list as group list</h1>
    <ul class="list-group">
        <li class="list-group-item">An item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A second item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A third item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A fourth item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">And a fifth one</li>
    </ul>

    <!--Add .active  indicate the current active selection.-->
    <h1 class="mt-2">.active indicate the current active selection</h1>
    <ul class="list-group">
        <li class="list-group-item active" aria-current="true">An active item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A second item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A third item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A fourth item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">And a fifth one</li>
    </ul>


    <!-- Replace <li> with <a> or <button> to make list items clickable. -->
    <h1 class="mt-2">we can add link in list-group</h1>
    <div class="list-group">
        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action active" aria-current="true">
            The current link item
        </a>
        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">A second link item</a>
        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">A third link item</a>
        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">A fourth link item</a>
        <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action disabled" aria-disabled="true">A disabled link item</a>
    </div>

    <!-- Replace <li> with <a> or <button> to make button items clickable. -->
    <h1 class="mt-2">we can add button in list-group</h1>
    <div class="list-group">
        <button type="button" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action active" aria-current="true">
            The current button
        </button>
        <button type="button" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">A second button item</button>
        <button type="button" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">A third button item</button>
        <button type="button" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action">A fourth button item</button>
        <button type="button" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action" disabled>A disabled button item</button>
    </div>

    <!--    flush can remove border from list-group-->
    <!-- Add .list-group-flush to remove some borders and rounded corners to render list group items edge-to-edge in a parent container (e.g., cards). -->
    <h1 class="mt-2">List group using flush</h1>
    <ul class="list-group list-group-flush">
        <li class="list-group-item">An item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A second item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A third item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A fourth item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">And a fifth one</li>
    </ul>


    <!--    Add the .list-group-numbered modifier class (and optionally use an <ol> element) to opt into numbered list group items.-->
    <!--    we can add number in list automatically-->
    <h1 class="mt-2">List group with number</h1>
    <ol class="list-group list-group-numbered">
        <li class="list-group-item">A list item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A list item</li>
        <li class="list-group-item">A list item</li>
    </ol>

    <!--    We can make list group as horizontal-->
    <!--    Add .list-group-horizontal to change the layout of list group items from vertical to horizontal across all breakpoints.-->

        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action list-group-item-warning">A simple warning list group
            item</a>
        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action list-group-item-info">A simple info list group
            item</a>

            item</a>
        <a href="#" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action list-group-item-dark">A simple dark list group
            item</a>
    </div>

---------------------------------------------------------------------------(3.5 )5. Forms & Input----------------------------------------------------------
.form-control(input,textarea,select এ বিভিন্ন styling করতে ব্যবহৃত হয়।)
	when to use:
	The .form-control class is used for the following form elements:
	
	Features:
		Adds consistent padding, border, and font size.

		Makes inputs responsive and visually appealing.

	<input> (e.g., type="text", type="email", type="password", etc.)

	<textarea>

	<select> (dropdowns)
	example:
	<input type="text" class="form-control" placeholder="Enter your name">

form-label:(label গুলো styling/designing এর জন্য form-level ব্যবহৃত হয়।)
	Purpose: Styles labels for form controls.

	Features:
		Improves accessibility by associating labels with inputs.

		Adds proper spacing and alignment.
		
	<input type="text" class="form-control" placeholder="Enter your name">

.form-text:(input field এর নীচে text/hint view করার জন্য এটা ব্যবহৃত হয়।)

	Used for adding helper text below form controls.
	
	Purpose: Styles helper text below form controls.

	Features:

		Used for additional instructions or validation messages.


<label>:
		Ensure the for attribute matches the id of the associated form control.(label এর for এবং input এর id match হতে হবে।)
		<div class="mb-3">
            <label for="exampleFormControlInput1" class="form-label">Email address</label>
            <input type="email" class="form-control" id="exampleFormControlInput1" placeholder="Enter your email">
        </div>

Properties for <input>:
	a. type
		Purpose: Defines the type of input.

		Common Types:

		text: Single-line text input.

		password: Masked input for passwords.

		email: Input for email addresses (validates format).

		number: Input for numeric values.

		date: Input for selecting a date.

		file: Input for file uploads.

		checkbox: For toggling options.

		radio: For selecting one option from a group.
		
	b. id
		Purpose: Uniquely identifies the input for association with <label>.
		
		<input type="text" id="username" name="username" class="form-control">
	
	c. name
		Purpose: Identifies the input when the form is submitted.
		
	d. placeholder
		Purpose: Provides a hint or example for the input.
	
	e. required
		Purpose: Marks the input as mandatory.
		
	f.min, max, and step
		Purpose: Used for numeric or date inputs to set constraints.
	
	g. pattern
		Purpose: Specifies a regex pattern for validation.
		
	h. aria-* Attributes
		Purpose: Enhances accessibility.

form-select:

			<select class="form-select" id="selectDefault">
                <option selected>Open this select menu</option>
                <option value="1">One</option>
                <option value="2">Two</option>
                <option value="3">Three</option>
            </select>

checkbox and radio:

form-check:

	Always wrap checkboxes and radio buttons in a .form-check container for proper alignment and spacing.

.form-check-input:

	Applied to the <input> element to style it according to Bootstrap's design.

.form-check-label:

	Applied to the <label> element to ensure it aligns properly with the input.

.name Attribute for Radio Buttons:

	All radio buttons in the same group must share the same name attribute to ensure only one can be selected at a time.
	
	

form-check form-switch : ( checkbox কে toogle button বানালাম। )
	<div class="form-check form-switch">:

	The form-check class creates a container for the checkbox and label.

	The form-switch class modifies the container to display a toggle switch instead of a regular checkbox.

range(range select করা যায়।)

input group(label ও input field কে combine করা যায়।)

floating label(label কে floating করা যায়।)


+++++++++++++++++code++++++++++++++++++++
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport"
          content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, minimum-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css">
    <style>

    </style>
    <style>

    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h2>FORM Control Example</h2>
    <form>
        <!-- Email Input -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="exampleFormControlInput1" class="form-label">Email address</label>
            <input type="email" class="form-control" id="exampleFormControlInput1" placeholder="Enter your email">
        </div>

        <!-- Textarea -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="exampleFormControlTextarea1" class="form-label">Example textarea</label>
            <textarea class="form-control" id="exampleFormControlTextarea1" rows="3" placeholder="Enter your message"></textarea>
        </div>

        <!-- Password Input with Help Text -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="inputPassword5" class="form-label">Password</label>
            <input type="password" id="inputPassword5" class="form-control" placeholder="Enter your password" aria-describedby="passwordHelpBlock">
            <div id="passwordHelpBlock" class="form-text">
                Your password must be 8-20 characters long, contain letters and numbers, and must not contain spaces, special characters, or emoji.
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Readonly Input -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="readonlyInput" class="form-label">Readonly Input</label>
            <input class="form-control" type="text" value="Readonly input here..." id="readonlyInput" aria-label="readonly input example" readonly>
        </div>

        <!-- Readonly Plain Text Email -->
        <div class="mb-3 row">
            <label for="staticEmail" class="col-sm-2 col-form-label">Email</label>
            <div class="col-sm-10">
                <input type="text" readonly class="form-control-plaintext" id="staticEmail" value="email@example.com">
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- File Input (Single File) -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="formFile" class="form-label">Default file input example</label>
            <input class="form-control" type="file" id="formFile">
        </div>

        <!-- File Input (Multiple Files) -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="formFileMultiple" class="form-label">Multiple files input example</label>
            <input class="form-control" type="file" id="formFileMultiple" multiple>
        </div>

        <!-- Color Picker -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="exampleColorInput" class="form-label">Color picker</label>
            <input type="color" class="form-control form-control-color" id="exampleColorInput" value="#563d7c" title="Choose your color">
        </div>

        <!-- Datalist Input -->
        <div class="mb-3">
            <label for="exampleDataList" class="form-label">Datalist example</label>
            <input class="form-control" list="datalistOptions" id="exampleDataList" placeholder="Type to search...">
            <datalist id="datalistOptions">
                <option value="San Francisco">
                <option value="New York">
                <option value="Seattle">
                <option value="Los Angeles">
                <option value="Chicago">
            </datalist>
        </div>

        <!-- Submit Button -->
        <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Submit</button>
    </form>
</div>


<script src="assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>












------------------------------------- 7. Alerts & Progress Bars-------------------------------------

Base Alert: .alert, .alert-* (e.g., .alert-success)
alert:দিলে div টি alert box হবে , ‍alert-success দিলে alert color change হবে।

Links: .alert-link
(link এর color পরিবর্তন করা যাবে।)

Headings: .alert-heading
(এটা দিয়ে alert box এর মধ্যে Heading add করা যাবে।)

Icons: .d-flex, .align-items-center, .ms-*
(image icon add করার জন্য d-flex করা হয়েছে।)

Dismissible: .alert-dismissible, .fade, .show, .btn-close, data-bs-dismiss="alert"
(alert box dismiss/কাটা যাবে।)

Base Classes: .progress, .progress-bar

Width: .w-* (e.g., .w-25, .w-50)

Colors: .bg-* (e.g., .bg-success, .bg-danger)

	Class Name				Description
	.progress				Base class for the progress bar container.(container)
	.progress-bar			Base class for the progress bar itself (the filled part).(color part)
	.w-*					Sets the width of the progress bar (e.g., .w-25 for 25% width).
	.bg-*					Sets the background color of the progress bar (e.g., .bg-success).
	.text-dark				Sets the text color to dark (useful for light backgrounds).
	.overflow-visible		Ensures text inside the progress bar is visible (prevents clipping).(text এর লেখা visible করা)

Stripes: .progress-bar-striped

Animation: .progress-bar-animated

Height: style="height: *px;" or .h-*

Labels: .text-dark, .overflow-visible

Accessibility: role="progressbar", aria-valuenow, aria-valuemin, aria-valuemax
+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++progress code++++++++++++++++++++++++++

        <div class="progress-bar" style="width: 0%"></div>

        <div class="progress-bar" style="width: 25%"></div>
    </div>

    </div>

    </div>

        <div class="progress-bar bg-success" style="width: 25%">25%</div>
    </div>

    </div>

-----------------------------------------------(3.8) 8. Tables------------------------------------------------------------

<!-- Defines the table structure -->
<table>

<!-- Groups the header content of the table -->
<thead>

<!-- Defines a table row -->
<tr>

<!-- Defines a header cell -->
<th>

<!-- Defines a standard data cell -->
<td>

.table:(bootstrap table apply করার জন্য table ব্যবহার করব।)

	Base class for Bootstrap tables.

	Adds default styling (padding, alignment, etc.).

.table-striped:(alternating row color এর জন্য table-striped ব্যবহার হয়।)

	Adds zebra-striping (alternating row colors) for better readability.

.table-bordered:(table এ bordere দেয়া যায়।)

	Adds borders to the table and its cells.

.table-borderless:

	Removes all borders from the table and its cells.

.table-dark:(table/tr/td তে বিভিন্ন color ব্যবহার করা যায়।)

	Inverts the table colors (dark background with light text).

.table-hover:

	Adds a hover effect to table rows (changes background color on hover).

.table-sm/md/lg/xl/xxl:

	Reduces padding, making the table more compact.

.table-responsive:(table কে responsive করতে চাইলে div এর ভিতরে table ব্যবহার করতে হবে।)

	Makes the table horizontally scrollable on smaller screens.

	Applied to a <div> wrapper around the table.

Contextual Classes:

.table-primary, .table-success, .table-danger, .table-warning, .table-info, .table-light, .table-dark.

	Used to color rows, cells, or headers based on their state or meaning.

Vertical Alignment Classes:(table এর ভিতরের cell data গুলো align করতে চাইলে align-top/middle/center ব্যবহার করতে হয়)

	.align-top: Aligns content to the top of the cell.

	.align-middle: Aligns content to the middle of the cell.

	.align-bottom: Aligns content to the bottom of the cell.

Width Utilities:(column এর width দেয়া যায়।)

	.w-25, .w-50, .w-75, .w-100: Sets the width of table columns.
















<!doctype html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport"
          content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, minimum-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="assets/css/bootstrap.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">
    <style>

    </style>
    <style>

    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h1 class="mb-1">Basic Table With table class</h1>
    <!-- Basic Tables -->
    <table class="table"> <!-- Table structure with Bootstrap styling -->
        <thead> <!-- Table header section -->
            <tr> <!-- Header row -->
                <th>#</th> <!-- Header cell for column 1 -->
                <th>Name</th> <!-- Header cell for column 2 -->
                <th>Email</th> <!-- Header cell for column 3 -->
                <th>Position</th> <!-- Header cell for column 4 -->
            </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody> <!-- Table body section -->
            <tr> <!-- First row of data -->
                <th>1</th> <!-- Row header cell (labels the row) -->
                <td>Tony Stark</td> <!-- Data cell for Name -->
                <td>ironman@gmail.com</td> <!-- Data cell for Email -->
                <td>Senior Web Developer</td> <!-- Data cell for Position -->
            </tr>
            <tr> <!-- Second row of data -->
                <th>2</th> <!-- Row header cell -->
                <td>Steve Rogers</td> <!-- Data cell for Name -->
                <td>captain@gmail.com</td> <!-- Data cell for Email -->
                <td>UI Designer</td> <!-- Data cell for Position -->
            </tr>
            <tr> <!-- Third row of data -->
                <th>3</th> <!-- Row header cell -->
                <td>Bruce Banner</td> <!-- Data cell for Name -->
                <td>hulk@gmail.com</td> <!-- Data cell for Email -->

                <td>This cell inherits <code>vertical-align: middle;</code> from the table</td>
                <td>This cell inherits <code>vertical-align: middle;</code> from the table</td>
                <td class="align-top">This cell is aligned to the top.</td> <!-- Data cell with top alignment -->
                <td>This here is some placeholder text, intended to take up quite a bit of vertical space,
                    to demonstrate how the vertical alignment works in the preceding cells.</td>

-------------------------------------------------(4.1) 1. Dropdowns------------------------------------------------------------


.dropdown: Wrapper class for creating a dropdown component.

.dropdown-toggle: Class for the button that toggles the dropdown menu.

.dropdown-menu: Class for the container of dropdown items.

.dropdown-item: Class for individual items inside the dropdown menu.

.btn-group: Class for grouping buttons, used in split dropdowns.

.dropdown-toggle-split: Class for the split button's dropdown arrow.

.dropdown-menu-dark: Class for applying a dark theme to the dropdown menu.

.dropup: Class for making the dropdown open upwards instead of downwards.

.visually-hidden: Class for hiding text visually while keeping it accessible to screen readers.

.btn: Base class for styling buttons (e.g., primary, danger, dark).

Single Button Dropdown: A basic dropdown with a single button that toggles the dropdown menu.

Split Button Dropdown: A dropdown with a split button, where one part is the primary action and the other part toggles the dropdown.

Dark Theme Dropdown: A dropdown with a dark-themed menu.

Dropup: A dropdown that opens upwards instead of downwards.

Bootstrap JavaScript bundle: The script that enables Bootstrap's interactive components, including dropdowns.


<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Dropdowns</title>
</head>
<body>

<!--Explanation of Comments:
Single Button Dropdown: A basic dropdown with a single button that toggles the dropdown menu.

Split Button Dropdown: A dropdown with a split button, where one part is the primary action and the other part toggles the dropdown.

Dark Theme Dropdown: A dropdown with a dark-themed menu.

Dropup: A dropdown that opens upwards instead of downwards.

Bootstrap JavaScript bundle: The script that enables Bootstrap's interactive components, including dropdowns.-->
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Dropdowns</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h1 class="mb-5">Dropdowns</h1>

    <!-- Single Button Dropdown -->
    <div class="dropdown">
        <!-- Dropdown toggle button -->
        <button
                class="btn btn-primary dropdown-toggle"
                data-bs-toggle="dropdown"
        >
            Dropdown
        </button>
        <!-- Dropdown menu with items -->
        <ul class="dropdown-menu">
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 1</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 2</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 3</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Split Button Dropdown -->
    <div class="btn-group">
        <!-- Primary action button -->
        <button class="btn btn-danger">Action</button>
        <!-- Dropdown toggle button (split) -->
        <button
                class="btn btn-danger dropdown-toggle dropdown-toggle-split"
                data-bs-toggle="dropdown"
        >
            <!-- Visually hidden text for accessibility -->
            <span class="visually-hidden">Toggle Dropdown</span>
        </button>
        <!-- Dropdown menu with items -->
        <ul class="dropdown-menu">
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 1</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 2</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 3</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Dark Theme Dropdown -->
    <div class="dropdown">
        <!-- Dropdown toggle button -->
        <button
                class="btn btn-primary dropdown-toggle"
                data-bs-toggle="dropdown"
        >
            Dropdown
        </button>
        <!-- Dropdown menu with dark theme -->
        <ul class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-dark">
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 1</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 2</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 3</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Dropup (Dropdown that opens upwards) -->
    <div class="btn-group dropup">
        <!-- Dropup toggle button -->
        <button class="btn btn-dark dropdown-toggle" data-bs-toggle="dropdown">
            Dropup
        </button>
        <!-- Dropup menu with dark theme -->
        <ul class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-dark">
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 1</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 2</a></li>
            <li><a href="#" class="dropdown-item">Item 3</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>

    <br /><br />

    <!-- Don't go past here -->
</div>
<div style="margin-top: 350px"></div>

<!-- Bootstrap JavaScript bundle -->
<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

-------------------------------------------(4.2)  2. Accordions & Collapse-----------------------------------------------------
Main Accordion Container:(এটাই parent container , এর মধ্যে মূলত সব ডাটা থাকবে।)

	The .accordion class is the wrapper for the entire accordion component.

	The id="accordionExample" is used to group the accordion items together.

Accordion Item:(এটা দিয়ে individual item গুলো নিয়ে কাজ করা হয়।)

	Each .accordion-item represents a single section of the accordion.

Accordion Header:(individual item এর header যেখানে button থাকে )

	The .accordion-header contains the toggle button (.accordion-button) for expanding/collapsing the content.

Toggle Button:(এর মাধ্যমে collapse/expand enable হয় এবং data-bs-target দ্বারা কি document show হবে তা select করা যায়।)

	The .accordion-button is the clickable button that toggles the visibility of the associated .accordion-collapse element.

	The data-bs-toggle="collapse" enables the collapse/expand functionality.

	The data-bs-target links the button to the specific collapsible element (e.g., #collapseOne).

Collapsible Content Area:(যে ডাটাগুলো show হবে তার container। .show class ব্যবহার করলে show/expanded থাকবে ।)

	The .accordion-collapse class is used for the collapsible content area.

	The .collapse class hides the content by default, and .show makes it visible (used for the first item in this example).

	The data-bs-parent ensures only one accordion item is open at a time (optional).

Accordion Body:(যেখানে ডাটা show হবে।)

	The .accordion-body class is used for the content inside the collapsible area.

কিভাবে accordion গুলো expanded রাখা যায় চাইলে।
<div id="collapseOne" class="accordion-collapse collapse show" data-bs-parent="#accordionExample"> 
এখান থেকে data-bs-parent উঠায় দিব।
<div id="collapseOne" class="accordion-collapse collapse show" data-bs-parent="#accordionExample"> 
where multiple items can stay open simultaneously), you need to remove the data-bs-parent attribute from the .accordion-collapse elements.





++++++++++++++++++++++++code++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Accordion & Collapse</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h1 class="mb-5">Accordion & Collapse</h1>
    <!-- Main Accordion Container -->
    <div class="accordion" id="accordionExample">

        <!-- First Accordion Item -->
        <div class="accordion-item">
            <!-- Accordion Header (contains the toggle button) -->
            <h2 class="accordion-header" id="headingOne">
                <!-- Toggle Button for the first item -->
                <button class="accordion-button" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#collapseOne">
                    Accordion Item #1
                </button>
            </h2>
            <!-- Collapsible Content Area for the first item -->
            <div id="collapseOne" class="accordion-collapse collapse show" data-bs-parent="#accordionExample">
                <!-- Content inside the collapsible area -->
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    Content for the first accordion item.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Second Accordion Item -->
        <div class="accordion-item">
            <!-- Accordion Header (contains the toggle button) -->
            <h2 class="accordion-header" id="headingTwo">
                <!-- Toggle Button for the second item (initially collapsed) -->
                <button class="accordion-button collapsed" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#collapseTwo">
                    Accordion Item #2
                </button>
            </h2>
            <!-- Collapsible Content Area for the second item -->
            <div id="collapseTwo" class="accordion-collapse collapse" data-bs-parent="#accordionExample">
                <!-- Content inside the collapsible area -->
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    Content for the second accordion item.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <!-- Third Accordion Item -->
        <div class="accordion-item">
            <!-- Accordion Header (contains the toggle button) -->
            <h2 class="accordion-header" id="headingThree">
                <!-- Toggle Button for the second item (initially collapsed) -->
                <button class="accordion-button collapsed" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#collapseThree">
                    Accordion Item #2
                </button>
            </h2>
            <!-- Collapsible Content Area for the second item -->
            <div id="collapseThree" class="accordion-collapse collapse" data-bs-parent="#accordionExample">
                <!-- Content inside the collapsible area -->
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    Content for the third accordion item.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

    </div>


    <h1 class="mb-5">Always-Open Accordion</h1>
    <!-- Main Accordion Container -->
    <div class="accordion" id="accordionExampleAlwaysShow">

        <!-- First Accordion Item -->
        <div class="accordion-item">
            <!-- Accordion Header (contains the toggle button) -->
            <h2 class="accordion-header" id="heading_1">
                <!-- Toggle Button for the first item -->
                <button class="accordion-button" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#collapse_1">
                    Accordion Item #1
                </button>
            </h2>
            <!-- Collapsible Content Area for the first item -->
            <div id="collapse_1" class="accordion-collapse collapse show">
                <!-- Content inside the collapsible area -->
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    Content for the first accordion item.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Second Accordion Item -->
        <div class="accordion-item">
            <!-- Accordion Header (contains the toggle button) -->
            <h2 class="accordion-header" id="heading_2">
                <!-- Toggle Button for the second item (initially collapsed) -->
                <button class="accordion-button collapsed" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#collapse_2">
                    Accordion Item #3
                </button>
            </h2>
            <!-- Collapsible Content Area for the second item -->
            <div id="collapse_2" class="accordion-collapse collapse">
                <!-- Content inside the collapsible area -->
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    Content for the third accordion item.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <!-- Third Accordion Item -->
        <div class="accordion-item">
            <!-- Accordion Header (contains the toggle button) -->
            <h2 class="accordion-header" id="heading_3">
                <!-- Toggle Button for the second item (initially collapsed) -->
                <button class="accordion-button collapsed" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#collapse_3">
                    Accordion Item #3
                </button>
            </h2>
            <!-- Collapsible Content Area for the second item -->
            <div id="collapse_3" class="accordion-collapse collapse">
                <!-- Content inside the collapsible area -->
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    Content for the third accordion item.
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

    </div>

    <!-- Don't go past here -->
</div>
<div style="margin-top: 350px"></div>

<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>



























-------------------------------------------(4.4)  4. Toast -----------------------------------------------------

.toast	Main container for the toast.(Main container)
.toast-header	Header section of the toast (title, timestamp, close button).(Header)
.toast-body	Main content of the toast.(Toast এর বডি)
.btn-close	Close button to dismiss the toast.(যেটা দিয়ে close হবে।)
.show	Makes the toast visible.(show না দিলে hidden থাকবে।)
.hide	Hides the toast.(Defaultly hidden থাকবে।)
.fade	Adds a fade animation to the toast.
.toast-container	Container for positioning multiple toasts.(একাধিক toast show করার জন্য toast-container use করতে হবে।)
Positioning Classes	Used to position the toast container (e.g., .top-0, .end-0).(positioning ঠিক করা যাবে।)

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark"> <!-- Sets the theme to dark mode -->
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" /> <!-- Ensures compatibility with IE -->
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" /> <!-- Responsive viewport settings -->
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" /> <!-- Links Bootstrap CSS -->
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Accordion & Collapse</title> <!-- Page title -->
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <h1>Basic Toast</h1>
    <!-- Basic toast example -->
    <div class="toast show" role="alert" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true">
        <!-- `toast` class initializes the toast component -->
        <!-- `show` class makes the toast visible by default -->
        <!-- `role`, `aria-live`, and `aria-atomic` attributes ensure accessibility -->
        <div class="toast-header">
            <!-- `toast-header` class styles the header section of the toast -->
            <img src="public/image/app-store.png" class="rounded me-2" style="width: 20px; height: 20px;" alt="...">
            <!-- `rounded` class adds rounded corners to the image -->
            <!-- `me-2` class adds margin to the right of the image -->
            <strong class="me-auto">Bootstrap</strong>
            <!-- `me-auto` class pushes the following elements to the right -->
            <small>11 mins ago</small>
            <!-- Displays a timestamp -->
            <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="toast" aria-label="Close"></button>
            <!-- `btn-close` class styles the close button -->
            <!-- `data-bs-dismiss="toast"` enables the close functionality -->
        </div>
        <div class="toast-body">
            <!-- `toast-body` class styles the body section of the toast -->
            Hello, world! This is a toast message.
        </div>
    </div>

    <h1>Toast Showing With Button (Position Fixed End 0 Bottom 0)</h1>
    <!-- Button to trigger the toast -->
    <button type="button" class="btn btn-primary" id="liveToastBtn">Show live toast</button>
    <!-- `btn btn-primary` styles the button -->

    <!-- Toast container positioned at the bottom-right corner -->
    <div class="toast-container position-fixed bottom-0 end-0 p-3">
        <!-- `toast-container` class groups multiple toasts -->
        <!-- `position-fixed` positions the container fixed on the screen -->
        <!-- `bottom-0` and `end-0` place the container at the bottom-right corner -->
        <!-- `p-3` adds padding around the container -->
        <div id="liveToast" class="toast" role="alert" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true">
            <!-- Toast with an ID for JavaScript interaction -->
            <div class="toast-header">
                <img src="public/image/app-store.png" class="rounded me-2" style="width: 20px; height: 20px;" alt="...">
                <strong class="me-auto">Bootstrap</strong>
                <small>11 mins ago</small>
                <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="toast" aria-label="Close"></button>
            </div>
            <div class="toast-body">
                Hello, world! This is a toast message.
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <h1>Stack Toast One Above Other</h1>
    <!-- Stacked toasts example -->
    <div class="toast-container position-static">
        <!-- `position-static` ensures the container does not use fixed positioning -->
        <div class="toast show" role="alert" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true">
            <!-- First toast -->
            <div class="toast-header">
                <img src="public/image/app-store.png" class="rounded me-2" style="width: 20px; height: 20px;" alt="...">
                <strong class="me-auto">Bootstrap</strong>
                <small class="text-body-secondary">just now</small>
                <!-- `text-body-secondary` class styles the text with a secondary color -->
                <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="toast" aria-label="Close"></button>
            </div>
            <div class="toast-body">
                See? Just like this.
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="toast show" role="alert" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true">
            <!-- Second toast -->
            <div class="toast-header">
                <img src="public/image/app-store.png" class="rounded me-2" style="width: 20px; height: 20px;" alt="...">
                <strong class="me-auto">Bootstrap</strong>
                <small class="text-body-secondary">2 seconds ago</small>
                <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="toast" aria-label="Close"></button>
            </div>
            <div class="toast-body">
                Heads up, toasts will stack automatically
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script> <!-- Links Bootstrap JS -->
<script>
    // JavaScript to handle toast display on button click
    const toastTrigger = document.getElementById('liveToastBtn'); // Gets the button element
    const toastLiveExample = document.getElementById('liveToast'); // Gets the toast element

    if (toastTrigger) {
        const toastBootstrap = bootstrap.Toast.getOrCreateInstance(toastLiveExample); // Initializes the toast
        toastTrigger.addEventListener('click', () => {
            toastBootstrap.show(); // Shows the toast when the button is clicked
        });
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>















---------------------------------------4.5 (5) 5. Spinners----------------------------------------------------==

Spinner Types
	.spinner-border: For a border spinner (default).
	.spinner-grow: For a growing spinner.
Sizing
	.spinner-border-sm: Small size for the border spinner.
	.spinner-grow-sm: Small size for the growing spinner.
Color Variants (Utility Classes)

	.text-primary
	.text-secondary
	.text-success
	.text-danger
	.text-warning
	.text-info
	.text-light
	.text-dark
	
Flex Alignment Utilities
	.d-flex: Makes the container a flexbox.
	.justify-content-center: Center the spinner horizontally.
	.align-items-center: Center the spinner vertically.
	


+++++++++++++++++++++++++code+++++++++++++++++++++++++++

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" />
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Accordion & Collapse</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container mt-5">
    <h1>---------------------Border Spinner (Default)------------------------</h1>
    <!-- Default border spinner -->
    <div class="spinner-border" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>

    <h1>---------------------Growing Spinner------------------------</h1>
    <!-- Growing spinner with secondary color -->
    <div class="spinner-grow text-secondary" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>

    <h1>------------------Small Border Spinner (Color Also)---------------------</h1>
    <!-- Small border spinner with danger color -->
    <div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-danger" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>

    <h1>-------------------Large Growing Spinner (Color Also)---------------------</h1>
    <!-- Large growing spinner without color -->
    <div class="spinner-grow spinner-grow-lg" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>
    <!-- Large growing spinner with danger color -->
    <div class="spinner-grow spinner-grow-lg text-danger" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>

    <h1>-------------------Spinner in d-flex ---------------------</h1>
    <!-- Spinner inside a flex container with border and padding -->
    <div class="d-flex align-items-center border border-danger rounded px-3 py-3">
        <strong role="status">Loading...</strong>
        <!-- Spinner aligned to the right -->
        <div class="spinner-border ms-auto" aria-hidden="true"></div>
    </div>

    <h1>-------------------Spinner Size ---------------------</h1>
    <!-- Custom size border spinner -->
    <div class="spinner-border" style="width: 3rem; height: 3rem;" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>
    <!-- Custom size growing spinner -->
    <div class="spinner-grow" style="width: 3rem; height: 3rem;" role="status">
        <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
    </div>
</div>



<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

---------------------------------------------------------4.7 7 popover button-----------------------------------------

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark"> <!-- Enables Bootstrap's dark mode -->
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" /> <!-- Link Bootstrap CSS -->
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Accordion & Collapse</title>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container mt-5"> <!-- Bootstrap container for proper spacing and responsiveness -->
    <!-- Button with hoverable popover -->
    <button type="button" class="btn btn-lg btn-danger" id="hoverPopover"
            data-bs-toggle="popover" data-bs-trigger="hover"
            data-bs-title="Popover title"
            data-bs-content="And here's some amazing content. It's very engaging. Right?"
            onclick="toggleMessage()">
        Hover to show popover, Click to Toggle Message
    </button>
    <!--
        btn         -> Applies Bootstrap button styles.
        btn-lg      -> Increases button size (large).
        btn-danger  -> Gives the button a red (danger) color.
    -->

    <!-- Div to show/hide message -->
    <div id="messageDiv" class="mt-3 text-white fw-bold" style="display: none;"></div>
    <!--
        mt-3       -> Adds margin-top spacing (size 3).
        text-white -> Sets text color to white.
        fw-bold    -> Makes the text bold.
    -->
</div>

<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script> <!-- Loads Bootstrap JavaScript -->
<script>
    // Enable popover with hover trigger
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        var popoverTrigger = document.getElementById('hoverPopover');
        new bootstrap.Popover(popoverTrigger, {
            trigger: 'hover' // Enables popover to appear on hover
        });
    });

    // Function to toggle message visibility
    function toggleMessage() {
        var messageDiv = document.getElementById("messageDiv");

        if (messageDiv.style.display === "none" || messageDiv.innerText === "") {
            messageDiv.innerText = "Button Clicked! Here's the displayed message.";
            messageDiv.style.display = "block"; // Show message
        } else {
            messageDiv.style.display = "none"; // Hide message
        }
    }
</script>

</body>
</html>



+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++Tooltip+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-bs-theme="dark"> <!-- Enables Bootstrap's dark mode -->
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="./assets/css/bootstrap.min.css" /> <!-- Link Bootstrap CSS -->
    <title>Bootstrap Sandbox | Tooltips</title>

</head>
<body>

<div class="container mt-5">
    <h1>---------------------------- Tooltip in Text --------------------------------</h1>
    <p class="text-muted"> <!-- Changed class from "muted" to "text-muted" (correct Bootstrap class) -->
        Placeholder text to demonstrate some
        <a href="#" data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-title="Default tooltip">inline links</a> with tooltips.
        This is now just filler, no killer.
        Content placed here just to mimic the presence of
        <a href="#" data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-title="Another tooltip">real text</a>.
        And all that just to give you an idea of how tooltips would look when used in real-world situations.
        So hopefully you've now seen how
        <a href="#" data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-title="Another one here too">these tooltips on links</a>
        can work in practice, once you use them on
        <a href="#" data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-title="The last tip!">your own</a>
        site or project.
    </p>
    <h1>-----------------Tooltip in button---------------</h1>
    <button type="button" class="btn btn-secondary"
            data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-placement="top"
            data-bs-title="This top tooltip is themed via CSS variables.">
        Custom tooltip
    </button>
</div>

<script src="./assets/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script> <!-- Loads Bootstrap JavaScript -->
<script>
    // Enable all tooltips on the page
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        var tooltipTriggerList = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="tooltip"]'));
        var tooltipList = tooltipTriggerList.map(function (tooltipTriggerEl) {
            return new bootstrap.Tooltip(tooltipTriggerEl);
        });
    });
</script>

</body>
</html>

<!--Enable popover-->
<script>
    // Ensure the DOM is fully loaded before initializing popovers
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        const popoverTriggerList = document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="popover"]');
        const popoverList = [...popoverTriggerList].map(popoverTriggerEl =>
            new bootstrap.Popover(popoverTriggerEl, { container: 'body' })
        );
    });
</script>

<!-- Enable Popover -->
<script>
    // Ensure the DOM is fully loaded before initializing popovers
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        const popoverTriggerList = document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="popover"]'); // Select all elements with popover functionality
        const popoverList = [...popoverTriggerList].map(popoverTriggerEl =>
            new bootstrap.Popover(popoverTriggerEl, { container: 'body' }) // Initialize popovers and append them to the body
        );
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

	$ npm init
	This utility will walk you through creating a package.json file.
	It only covers the most common items, and tries to guess sensible defaults.

	See `npm help init` for definitive documentation on these fields
	and exactly what they do.

	Use `npm install <pkg>` afterwards to install a package and
	save it as a dependency in the package.json file.

	Press ^C at any time to quit.

	in package.json file sass added
		"dependencies": {
			"sass": "^1.85.0"
		  }



+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++create folder(project folder এ/root এ)+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
1.create folder scss
2.inside this folder create styles.scss file


+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++change in package.json file+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
"scripts": {
    "sass:build": "sass scss:css"
  },

This means you're telling Sass to compile all .scss files in the scss directory 
and output the compiled .css files into the css directory.
  
+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++now code scss format into styles.scss file+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
$primary:#333;
body{
  background-color: $primary;
}

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++now run sass compiler+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++

User@DESKTOP-CF95DK1 MINGW64 /c/xampp/htdocs/bs5-simple-starter
$ npm run sass:build

> bs5-simple-starter@1.0.0 sass:build
> sass --no-source-map scss:css


**(After this command folder will be created and file also creaed css/style.css)**
**in style.css file browser supported css file generated**


+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++now code into html file and link with css file+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport"
          content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, minimum-scale=1.0">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="ie=edge">
    <title>Document</title>
	 <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/styles.css">
</head>
<body>
    <h1>SASS INSTALL</h1>
</body>
</html>



+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++if you don't want styles.css.map file will not genearted+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
write in package.json file

 "scripts": {
    "sass:build": "sass --no-source-map scss:css"
  },
  
  
  


+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++if you don't want every time build than use watch+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
write in package.json file
	"scripts": {
	  "sass:build": "sass --no-source-map scss:css",
	  "sass:watch": "sass --no-source-map --watch scss:css"
	}
  
+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++now apply watch and further no need to build again and again+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++

User@DESKTOP-CF95DK1 MINGW64 /c/xampp/htdocs/bs5-simple-starter
$ npm run sass:watch

> bs5-simple-starter@1.0.0 sass:watch
> sass --no-source-map --watch scss:css

Sass is watching for changes. Press Ctrl-C to stop.

@import '../node_modules/@fortawesome/fontawesome-free/scss/brands.scss';
@import '../node_modules/@fortawesome/fontawesome-free/scss/solid.scss';

	5.npm install করব।
	
	User@DESKTOP-CF95DK1 MINGW64 /c/xampp/htdocs/Ebook_Website_Bootstrap
	$ npm install
	
	[npm init: Used to initialize a new Node.js project. It creates a package.json(npm init দিলে package.json install হবে।)
	
	npm install: Used to install packages (dependencies) for your project.(যত project dependency আছে সব install করবে।)
	It also creates a node_modules folder and a package-lock.json file if they don't exist.(npm install মূলত)
	If you have an existing package.json, just run npm install to install all listed dependencies.(package.json file আছে তাই npm install দিব।)]

            <span class="navbar-toggler-icon"></span>

            <!-- navbar in right  write regarding to your need ; make navbar responsive-->
            <!--
            m-auto: for Small screens (< md): <ul> place in center
            m-md-0: clear all margin; Overrides the m-auto class starting from the medium (md) breakpoint (≥ 768px), removing all margins.
            ms-md-auto: Applies a left align from the medium (md) breakpoint(>=768px),
            ms-md-auto: Applies a left align from the medium (md) breakpoint(>=768px),
            mb-2 : margin bottom for all screen size (here : for small screen(>=576px and <768px))
            mb-md-0 : for md screen(>=768px) margin bottom 0
            gap-1 : for all screen (here : for small screen(>=576px and <768px))
            gap-md-4 : for md screen(>=768px) gap-4-->

            <ul class="navbar-nav ms-auto">

------------------------------------------------------(7.6) 6. Navbar Scroll Effect-----------------------------
//add js
function userScroll() {
    const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');

    window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        if (window.scrollY > 50) {
            navbar.classList.add('bg-dark');
            navbar.classList.add('navbar-sticky');
        } else {
            navbar.classList.remove('bg-dark');
            navbar.classList.remove('navbar-sticky');
        }
    });
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', userScroll);


//add style.scss for transition effect (ease-in-ease-out)
.navbar {
  transition: all 0.5s ease-in-out;
}

.navbar-sticky {
  opacity: 0.9;
  box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5);
}

//style.scss(increase iframe size)
.map iframe {
  left: 0;
  top: 0;
  height: 400px;
  width: 100%;
  border: none;
}



//work in contact.html
//how to create iframe for google map
Go to Google Maps: Open Google Maps and search for the location you want to embed.

Share the Map: Click on the menu button (three horizontal lines) in the top-left corner, then click on "Share or embed map."

Choose the Embed Option: In the dialog that appears, select the "Embed a map" tab.

Copy the iframe Code: You'll see an <iframe> code snippet. Copy it.

Paste the Code: Paste the copied <iframe> code into your HTML file where you want the map to appear.

----------------------------------------------------(7.10) 10. Deploy To Vercel---------------------------------------------
(serach video: How To Deploy GitHub Project on Vercel (Step By Step))
1. go to vercel
https://vercel.com/

2.login with githube

3.install git repository(first time)

4.only select repository option

5.import github repository

6.build command for saas
	npm run build:sass
7.deploy







---------------------------------------------(7.11) 11. Formspree For Contact Forms---------------------------------------------

https://formspree.io/

1.create form in this website 

2.we will get link( https://formspree.io/f/mnnjoznb)

3.put this link in form
	 <form action="https://formspree.io/f/mnnjoznb" method="post">
	 
4.we can get submitted data into this website













































---------------------------------------------8 Website 2 - Corso Training Website------------------------------------

---------------------------------------------(8.2) 2. Project Setup (bootstrap.scss এ যেসকল ‍adjustment করতে হবে সেগুলো set করব।)-------------------------------------------------
1.create folder name C:\xampp\htdocs\corso-website-final

2.copy C:\xampp\htdocs\SAAS_SETUP data to our project folder

3.in index.html we link all of our resources
 and we add googlefont also(montserrat)(https://fonts.google.com/)
  <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Montserrat:ital,wght@0,100..900;1,100..900&display=swap"
        rel="stylesheet">
		

4.now we open terminal in phpstrome
    User@DESKTOP-CF95DK1 MINGW64 /c/xampp/htdocs/Ebook_Website_Bootstrap
	$ npm install
	
	
	User@DESKTOP-CF95DK1 MINGW64 /c/xampp/htdocs/Ebook_Website_Bootstrap
	$ npm run sass:watch



5.We need to set font in bootstrap.scss file
// Font Set
$font-family-sans-serif: 'Montserrat', sans-serif;
  
//Color set

$primary: #f8b547;
$secondary: #35353a;
$light: #fbf9f5;
$body-bg: $light;



// Spacing Set(Add extra space ; we can use mt-6/7/8)
$spacer: 1rem !default;
$spacers: (
        0: 0,
        1: $spacer * 0.25,
        2: $spacer * 0.5,
        3: $spacer,
        4: $spacer * 1.5,
        5: $spacer * 3,
        6: $spacer * 6,
        7: $spacer * 8,
        8: $spacer * 12,
) !default;



//Purpose: This variable sets the bottom margin for all heading elements (<h1> to <h6>).
//h1 to h6 ব্যবহার করলে extra space নিবে নীচে।
//defaultly দেয়া .5rem: //$headings-margin-bottom:      $spacer * .5 !default;
$headings-margin-bottom: $spacer * 1;


//This variable sets the base line height for the entire document. Line height controls the vertical spacing between lines of text.
//প্রত্যেক লাইন এর মধ্যে space বাড়ায় দিবে।
$line-height-base: 1.7;

// Navbar এর ‍space adjust করব।
$navbar-nav-link-padding-x: 0.8rem; // Horizontal padding for navbar links (left and right).
$navbar-padding-y: 1rem; // Vertical padding for the navbar (top and bottom).
$navbar-dark-color: #fff; // Text color for dark-themed navbars (white by default).


// Buttons radius and padding adjustment
$button-radius: 50px;
$button-padding-x: 30px;
$button-padding-y: 10px;

$btn-border-radius: $button-radius;
$btn-border-radius-sm: $button-radius;
$btn-border-radius-lg: $button-radius;
$btn-padding-y: $button-padding-y;
$btn-padding-y-lg: $button-padding-y;
$btn-padding-y-sm: $button-padding-y;
$btn-padding-x: $button-padding-x;
$btn-padding-x-lg: $button-padding-x;
$btn-padding-x-sm: $button-padding-x;
$navbar-toggler-border-radius: 5px;



//toggler button radius change not 50px we want 5px
$navbar-toggler-border-radius: 5px;

//heading font increase
$headings-font-weight: bold;

//hero slide width reduce
.hero .slide{
  width: 70%;
  margin: 0 auto;
}





<!--Header-->
<!-- Header Section -->
<div class="header">
    <!-- Hero Section with Full-Screen Height -->
    <div class="hero py-7 vh-100"> <!-- py-7: Vertical padding, vh-100: Full viewport height -->
        <div class="container"> <!-- Bootstrap container for centering content -->
            <!--Slide/Carousel-->
            <!-- Slide/Carousel Section -->
            <div class="row"> <!-- Creates a Bootstrap row for layout -->
                <div class="col-12"> <!-- Full-width column to hold the carousel -->

                    <!-- Image Slider -->
                    <div id="slider" class="carousel slide"> <!-- Bootstrap carousel with sliding transition -->

                        <!-- Carousel Indicators (Dots) -->
                        <!--'active' makes this the default slide-->
                        <div class="carousel-indicators">
                            <button type="button"
                                    data-bs-target="#slider"
                                    data-bs-slide-to="0"
                                    class="active"
                                    aria-current="true"
                                    aria-label="Slide 1">
                            </button>
                            <button type="button"
                                    data-bs-target="#slider"
                                    data-bs-slide-to="1"
                                    aria-label="Slide 2">
                            </button>
                            <button type="button"
                                    data-bs-target="#slider"
                                    data-bs-slide-to="2"
                                    aria-label="Slide 3">
                            </button>
                        </div>

                        <!-- Carousel Inner Wrapper -->
                        <div class="carousel-inner rounded-5"> <!-- 'rounded-5' applies large rounded corners -->

                            <!-- First Slide -->
                            <div class="carousel-item active"> <!-- 'carousel-item' defines a slide, 'active' makes it default -->
                                <img src="images/header-slide-1.jpg"
                                     class="d-block w-100 rounded-5"
                                alt="Slide 1"><!-- 'd-block' makes it a block element, 'w-100' makes it full width -->
                            </div>

                            <!-- Second Slide -->
                            <div class="carousel-item">
                                <img src="images/header-slide-2.jpg"
                                     class="d-block w-100 rounded-5"
                                     alt="Slide 2">
                            </div>

                            <!-- Third Slide -->
                            <div class="carousel-item">
                                <img src="images/header-slide-3.jpg"
                                     class="d-block w-100 rounded-5"
                                     alt="Slide 3">
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <!-- Previous Button -->
                        <button class="carousel-control-prev" type="button" data-bs-target="#slider"
                                data-bs-slide="prev">
                            <span class="carousel-control-prev-icon" aria-hidden="true"></span> <!-- Arrow icon for previous slide -->
                            <span class="visually-hidden">Previous</span> <!-- Hidden text for screen readers -->
                        </button>

                        <!-- Next Button -->
                        <button class="carousel-control-next" type="button" data-bs-target="#slider"
                                data-bs-slide="next">
                            <span class="carousel-control-next-icon" aria-hidden="true"></span> <!-- Arrow icon for next slide -->
                            <span class="visually-hidden">Next</span> <!-- Hidden text for screen readers -->
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
